None of these laws create missing candidates. The route must already be born by Muse and visible through Harvest/I2E candidate shelves.

## Final Gen Rebuild: Convergence Arbitration Layer

### Reason For This Entry

During the Final Gen rebuild, the system showed a repeated top-script weakness:

- Mind, Finder, and Edge could often recognize the right structural neighborhood,
- but HIGH/MAX mirrors and close sibling bodies were crowding the top seats,
- raw score was rewarding loudness, repetition, and clean-looking mirrors,
- quiet or MID survivor bodies could be structurally alive but underweighted after admission.

The discovery was named:

`Convergence`

Convergence is now documented in:

`Books Of The Lotto/Books Of Understanding/BOOK OF CONVERGENCE - Current Canonical Edition.md`

### Core Concept

The old ranking question was:

```text
Which candidate is strongest?
```

The new arbitration question is:

```text
Which candidate carries the correct amount of burden for this transition?
```

The key law is:

```text
Birth prefers sufficient pressure, not maximum pressure.
```

This matters because the winning body can be ugly but alive:

```text
burden -> compression -> distortion -> survival -> emergence
```

### Pipeline Placement

Convergence belongs after structure detection but before final ranking.

The intended flow is:

```text
Motion
-> Structure
-> Pressure family
-> Transition cost measurement
-> Emergence pressure matching
-> Candidate arbitration
-> Final ranking
```

In Final Gen order:

```text
IIW
-> Mind
-> Keys
-> Identity
-> Pre-Finder Domain/Convergence Gate
-> Finder
-> Edge
-> Full BDE / Finality
-> Genesis
-> Arrow
-> Historia
-> Muse
-> Harvest
-> I2E
```

### Diagnostic Breakthrough

The March 4-style miss exposed the mirror problem clearly.

For:

```text
2026-03-02 -> 2026-03-04
```

Target:

```text
Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | MID
```

Convergence read:

```text
CONVERGENT
```

But the close mirrors:

```text
Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | HIGH
Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | MAX
```

were read as:

```text
OVERPRESSURE
```

Lesson:

The target was not structurally impossible.
The higher-pressure mirrors were louder than the transition required.

### Second Breakthrough: Quiet Resolution

The first Convergence formula was too simple for compression bodies.

It could misread quiet compression as underpowered because it compared everything against hot pressure.

The repair split Convergence into two laws:

1. `Pressure Convergence`
2. `Resolution Convergence`

Pressure Convergence punishes inflated HIGH/MAX mirrors.

Resolution Convergence protects quiet compression bodies when the field is resolving pressure through contraction.

Examples requiring quiet-resolution logic:

```text
High-Mid | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MIN
Ext High-High | Canonical | COMPRESSION | ABSOLUTE ZERO
Mid-Low | Canonical | COMPRESSION | LOW
High-High | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MID
```

### Implementation Completed

Convergence was first tested in diagnostic form:

`Testing Items/_tmp_finalgen_convergence_diagnostic.py`

Then it was wired into the Final Gen top scripts as soft arbitration.

#### IIW

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Infinite_Inner_World.py`

New source metric:

`emergence_convergence_metric`

IIW now measures:

- `required_cost`
- `raw_required_cost`
- `structural_work`
- `quiet_resolution_need`
- `pressure_arbitration_need`
- `hot_overfavor_risk`
- `compression_need_score`
- `projection_high_max`
- `projection_low_mid`
- `motion_budget`
- `sorted_budget`
- `fp_shift`
- `sum_shift`
- `anchor_move`
- `cluster_state`
- `world_state`

This makes Convergence a measurable world metric, not only a downstream scoring idea.

#### Mind

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Judgement_Of_Mind.py`

Mind now reads IIW `emergence_convergence_metric` and writes candidate-level:

`emergence_convergence_profile`

Mind uses Convergence after structure detection and before final path ranking.

#### Keys

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Infinity's_Keeper_Of_Keys.py`

Keys now reads the IIW convergence room inside:

`key_path_agreement_profile`

Keys can now say whether the current key condition supports:

- quiet resolution,
- balanced emergence,
- hot pressure permission,
- hot overpressure caution.

#### Identity

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Banshees's_Birth_Identity.py`

Identity now emits:

`convergence_identity_profile`

Identity can now say whether the current body is:

- `BODY_SUPPORTS_QUIET_RESOLUTION`
- `BODY_SUPPORTS_PRESSURE`
- `BODY_REQUIRES_OVERPRESSURE_CAUTION`
- `BODY_NEUTRAL`

#### Finder

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Birth_Path_Finder.py`

Finder now consumes:

- Mind convergence profiles,
- Identity convergence body permission,
- the pre-Finder Domain/Convergence Gate.

Finder uses Convergence as a soft score and evidence signal.
It may not create a missing path from Convergence alone.

#### Pre-Finder Domain/Convergence Gate

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Metrica's_Domian_Expansion.py`

BDE has been split into two lawful positions:

1. `build_pre_finder_domain_gate(...)`
2. `build_birth_domain_expansion_packet(...)`

The pre-Finder gate runs after Identity and before Finder. It reads IIW Convergence, Mind, Keys, and Identity, then emits:

- `gate_mode`
- `domain_scores`
- `domain_policy`
- `finder_gate_policy`
- `domain_score_adjustments`
- `fp_band_score_adjustments`

This lets Finder see whether the live world is a hot-overfavor, quiet-resolution, pressure-arbitration, or balanced convergence field before the top seats are ranked.

The full BDE packet still runs after Edge. It remains the later domain aperture governor before Finality.

#### Edge

File:

`Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Eternity's_Edge.py`

Edge now carries Convergence into final pressure arbitration before downstream handoff.

### Current Diagnostic Result

After wiring:

- syntax checks passed for all Final Gen Python files,
- the convergence diagnostic ran successfully,
- `The_Final_Orchestrator.py` now runs the corrected front order through Finality,
- the active front order is now `IIW -> Mind -> Keys -> Identity -> Pre-Finder Domain/Convergence Gate -> Finder -> EdgePath -> Full BDE -> Finality`,
- `2026-02-21` currently reads `finder40=17`, `edge40=20`,
- `2026-05-02` remained correctly labeled `RESOLUTION_CONVERGENT`,
- March 4 remains an admission problem, not only an arbitration problem,
- March 9 remains a ranking-pressure problem with target still correctly labeled `CONVERGENT`.

### Order Power Comparison

The corrected front order was compared with and without the pre-Finder gate using:

`Testing Items/_tmp_finalgen_order_power_compare.py`

January through May 2026 target-path rank coverage showed:

- Mind baseline stayed unchanged because Mind runs before the gate.
- Finder top-10 stayed unchanged.
- Edge top-10 stayed unchanged.
- Finder top-20 improved by one total case across January-May.
- Edge top-20 improved by one total case across January-May.
- May improved from `finder_top20=6/7`, `edge_top20=6/7` to `finder_top20=7/7`, `edge_top20=7/7`.
- The key May movement was `2026-04-29 -> 2026-05-02`, where `High-High | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MID` moved from Finder `32` / Edge `26` to Finder `12` / Edge `12`.

The test also exposed an important safeguard:

- broad quiet-body boosting can flood the room,
- but quiet bodies that Mind already held alive need stronger seat protection inside hot-overfavor fields.

Finder now applies a narrower `mind_alive_quiet_body_seat_protection` only when the quiet body already has Mind evidence. This keeps April stable while preserving the May gain.

### Mind Handoff And Genesis Vote Ledger

The next correction was not to let every IIW projected body enter Mind. A direct `IIW_WORLD_PROJECTION` admission experiment was rejected because it flooded May with broad hot-family projection bodies and erased the useful `2026-05-02` quiet-resolution gain.

The safer law is:

- Mind must hand off a wider survival shelf.
- Downstream courts must keep their own vote visible through Finality.
- Genesis must receive a vote ledger, not only a raw Finality rank.

Implementation:

- `The_Final_Orchestrator.py` now builds Mind with `candidate_limit=40`.
- `Metrica's_Domian_Expansion.py` demo now builds Mind with `candidate_limit=40`.
- `Sora's_Finality.py` demo now builds Mind with `candidate_limit=40`.
- `Sora's_Finality.py` now emits `genesis_handoff_profile` for every candidate.
- Finality now emits `genesis_handoff_paths`.

The `genesis_handoff_profile` preserves:

- Mind rank,
- Finder rank,
- Edge rank,
- BDE domain permission,
- Finality status,
- a combined handoff score,
- handoff class.

This means Genesis can see how the whole front court voted instead of inheriting only a flattened finality list.

Current January-May check after this pass:

- January: stable.
- February: stable.
- March: one visibility gain; `2026-03-04` moves from missing to Finder `26` / Edge `32`.
- April: stable.
- May: keeps the top-20 gain; `2026-05-02` remains Finder `12` / Edge `12`.

This confirms the correct direction:

`Mind wider shelf -> Finder/Edge/BDE/Finality vote -> Genesis handoff ledger`

not:

`IIW broad projection -> Mind admission flood`.

### Important Constraint

Convergence is not a hard gate.

It is a soft arbitration layer.

It must not:

- inject target truth,
- rescue a date,
- use future draw data,
- replace Muse construction,
- replace Historia memory,
- override Finder sovereignty alone,
- reject strange survivor bodies just because they are not pretty.

### Relationship To Clone Suppression

The conversation also clarified that the top scripts need clone-family protection.

Clone suppression solves:

```text
Too many similar bodies take the top seats.
```

Convergence solves:

```text
The wrong burden magnitude takes the top seat.
```

The two should work together:

- deduplicate clone signatures,
- cap family crowding,
- penalize overlap,
- then use Convergence to decide which sibling carries lawful burden.

### Relationship To Inverted Spire

Inverted Spire is the only-if gate.

Convergence is the burden arbitration law.

Inverted Spire asks:

```text
May this candidate stand here?
```

Convergence asks:

```text
Does this candidate carry the right amount of burden?
```

### Current Open Problems

1. March 4-style bodies still need better admission.

The target can be `CONVERGENT`, but if Mind/Finder/Edge never admit the exact body, arbitration cannot save it.

2. Canonical expansion MAX needs its own permission law.

Some MAX bodies are inflated; some are lawful expansion releases.

3. Muse and Historia are not yet rebuilt around Convergence.

The top scripts now speak the language, but downstream route construction has not yet fully learned it.

4. Top-10 crowding still needs stronger family caps.

Convergence reduces pressure inflation, but clone/crowd controls still need to be applied carefully.

5. Historical coverage must separate:

- overpressure mirror cases,
- quiet resolution cases,
- lawful MAX rupture cases,
- admission misses,
- downstream construction misses,
- final-card authority misses.

### Law Going Forward

Future improvements must treat Convergence as measurable burden law:

```text
Motion measures behavior.
Structure measures form.
Pressure measures tension.
Mana measures transition cost.
Sorted Mana measures structural work.
Convergence arbitrates lawful burden.
```

The Final Gen rebuild should no longer reward the loudest mirror by default.

The system must reward the body that survives the measured transition workload.

## 2026-05-19 - Eternal Crystallized Affinite Birth Path Doctrine

The latest research moved the rebuild from base birth-path prediction into path-to-number-body construction.

The core realization:

```text
The numbers are the final physical expression.
The system must first understand what living body the path can lawfully wear.
```

Base birth path remains:

```text
set_type / arc / pressure / fp_band
```

But this is only the skeleton.

The new doctrine is:

```text
Eternal Crystallized Affinite Birth Path
= Base Birth Path
+ Crystallized Room Conditions
+ Eternal Seat/GAP/FP/SUM Life
+ Affinity Number Compatibility
```

### Documentation Added

A new canonical book was created:

```text
Books Of The Lotto/Books Of Understanding/Books Of Birth Paths/BOOK OF ETERNAL CRYSTALLIZED AFFINITE BIRTH PATH - Current Canonical Edition.md
```

The Book of Convergence was also expanded with:

- room archetypes,
- draw-to-draw residue,
- true MAX versus false MAX,
- quiet resolution inside loud rooms,
- May 2 -> May 4 diagnostic lesson,
- bridge-number problem,
- relationship to Eternal Crystallized Affinite Birth Path.

### Research Tools Added

The following diagnostic scripts were created:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_iiw_convergence_overflow_research.py
Testing Items/_tmp_iiw_convergence_room_archetypes.py
Testing Items/_tmp_iiw_convergence_draw_to_draw_trace.py
Testing Items/_tmp_iiw_metric_utilization_audit.py
Testing Items/_tmp_crystallized_birth_path_research.py
Testing Items/_tmp_crystallized_number_role_rehearsal.py
```

These scripts are research-only.

They do not alter rankings, inject answers, rescue dates, or select final combinations.

### What Was Learned

IIW is abstract future prediction.

It predicts:

```text
room workload
emergence cost
pressure debt
quiet resolution need
hot overfavor risk
residual burden
lawful body conditions
```

It does not directly predict exact numbers.

The safer architecture is:

```text
IIW reads room
Mind/Finder/Edge crystallize lawful path
Eternity/Niravna test life and corridors
Affinity tests number compatibility
Genesis/Arrow/Muse construct exact bodies
Harvest/E2I survive final bodies
```

### May 2 -> May 4 Diagnostic Result

Source:

```text
2026-05-02
25, 37, 42, 52, 65
High-High | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MID
```

Target:

```text
2026-05-04
30, 36, 42, 60, 63
High-High | Burst | SEPARATION | LOW
```

The target crystal from the May 2 room had:

```text
required_cost = 0.790313
pressure_arbitration_need = 0.63083
hot_overfavor_risk = 0.769807
FP corridor = 30-39
sum corridor = 176-269
court day = mirror_rejection
active day types = mirror_rejection, quiet_compression_survival
```

The actual May 4 draw:

```text
30, 36, 42, 60, 63
FP = 33
sum = 231
```

fit the target crystal.

Seat-role rehearsal also showed the actual numbers were role-visible:

```text
S1 = 30
S2 = 36
S3 = 42
S4 = 60
S5 = 63
```

The most important issue was `60`.

`60` was only a rank-9 S4 role candidate, but it was still a lawful high bridge.

This means exact-number construction can fail if Arrow or Muse only keeps the loudest isolated seat numbers.

The lesson is now explicit:

```text
The system must not confuse isolated seat loudness with lawful body necessity.
```

### New Open Problem

Eternity/Niravna and Affinity must evolve before Arrow/Muse can be trusted with exact construction.

The next needed work:

1. Eternity must recognize when a lower-ranked bridge number is necessary for gap life.
2. Affinity must understand number-to-number compatibility inside the crystallized path.
3. Arrow must rank seat authority without killing lawful bridge numbers too early.
4. Muse must construct full bodies from role-compatible seats, not isolated strong numbers.
5. Harvest must judge the complete living body, not only individual number strength.

### Updated Pipeline Direction

The rebuild should no longer ask only:

```text
Which birth path wins?
```

It must ask:

```text
What living number body can this lawful path wear?
```

This becomes the bridge from path prediction to exact-number construction.

## 2026-05-19 - Clairvoyance Aim Doctrine

Clairvoyance has been named and documented as the next research layer.

Book added:

```text
Books Of The Lotto/Books Of Understanding/BOOK OF CLAIRVOYANCE - Current Canonical Edition.md
```

Research script added:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_aim_research.py
```

Clairvoyance means sealed target aiming before the future draw is known.

It does not use the target draw to create candidates.
It forms an aim from Convergence, crystallized path evidence, room workload, court-day authority, FP/sum corridors, and number-role rehearsal.

The May 2 -> May 4 diagnostic showed the new split clearly:

```text
Raw aim overfavored Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | HIGH.
Mirror-rejection arbitration moved the aim to High-High | Burst | SEPARATION | LOW.
That was the actual May 4 birth path.
```

The corrected aim also reached the right broad numeric room:

```text
aim FP: about 30 inside 30-39
actual FP: 33

aim sum: about 239 inside 176-269
actual sum: 231
```

The remaining failure is exact number identity.

The system still chose nearby bodies that matched FP/sum pressure but missed the living exact body.

This proves the next research target:

```text
Clairvoyance can aim the room.
Eternity and Affinity must explain which exact numbers can live in that room together.
```

### Motion-First Clairvoyance Audit

The current correction changed Clairvoyance from sorted-heavy to motion-first.

The lawful reading order is now:

```text
Motion first -> sorted structure second -> Convergence -> crystallized path -> exact construction.
```

Clarification:

```text
57/57 = IIW packet usage coverage, not prediction accuracy.
24/57 = direct Clairvoyance field usage, not hit rate.
```

The first 2026 audit after motion-first and Boost/Form weighting:

```text
draws: 57
path top1: 6/57
path top3: 14/57
path top5: 19/57
path top10: 29/57
path top20: 44/57
aim FP corridor: 22/57
aim sum corridor: 51/57
```

This means Clairvoyance is not yet a top-1 oracle.

It is currently a narrowing court that can reduce the downstream prediction table, especially through sum corridor and top-20 crystallized path containment.

The next improvement target is FP corridor and arc arbitration, because the script still over-aims loud archetypes when motion is active.

### 2026-05-19 - Clairvoyance Flexible Memory Calibration

The latest Clairvoyance lesson is that rank-1 capability exists, but local calibration fades when stretched across the year.

Therefore the rebuild now uses month-sized and draw-sized calibration:

```text
one room at a time -> learn shape grammar -> test against another room -> keep only reusable laws
```

New diagnostic file:

```text

```

New report files:


Clairvoyance now has a modest Historia-style flexible memory score inside:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_aim_research.py
```

This memory reads:

- prior same-birth-path transitions,
- prior same-set-type transitions,
- prior same-arc transitions,
- target path component frequencies,
- set-style tendencies,
- FP bucket tendencies,
- era-weighted witness strength.

It may only act as context.

It may not:

- copy old numbers,
- lock to a date,
- lock to a year,
- rescue a target after the fact,
- force top 1 by one historical witness.

The remaining open problem is pressure/FP crystallization:

```text
When motion is loud, determine whether the lawful next body is truly HIGH/MAX/CRISIS
or whether the room only needs MID/LOW Burst/Separation to complete emergence.
```

The Motion side now uses the Motion books:

- Motion is draw-order first.
- Transitional is the native active-equilibrium field.
- Fatigued is retained pressure.
- Explosive is discharge.
- Directed is trend/one-way behavior.
- Calm is not the center, but it is a lawful low-energy state.
- Chaotic is unstable mixed rupture.

The sorted side now uses:

- Favors for structural body,
- Possibility for occupied field,
- Reduction for lawful narrowing,
- Sorted Memory for slot/corridor discipline,

### 2026-05-19 - Hybrid / Rules / Mana / Era Clairvoyance Foundation

The next research question was whether the Hybrid, Rules, Mana, Era, and Dynasty books should be added before the advanced Books of Understanding.

Current answer:

```text
Yes. They belong before the advanced techniques as world-foundation law.
```

The reason is architectural:

```text
Books of Understanding explain special techniques.
Hybrid / Rules / Mana / Era books explain the room those techniques must live inside.
```

Clairvoyance now treats these books as a foundation layer:

- Infinity: lawful universe, center, edge, sparse edge, dormant lawful edge.
- Form: hard contradiction, soft contradiction, agreement law.
- Affinities: compatibility and role fit.
- Transitions: handoff behavior rather than raw probability.
- Pressure: burden specificity and unstable handoff.
- Odds: field appetite among lawful outcomes.
- Master Ladder: diagnostic dominance only after the room is declared.
- Mana: transition cost.
- Sorted Mana: sorted structural work.
- Mana Era System: era hosts mana; era does not redefine mana.
- Dynasty/Era books: field hosting, era appetite, and dormant/active law.

Implementation:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_aim_research.py
```

New scoring support:

```text
ERA_FORM_HOSTS
ERA_TRAFFIC
DORMANT_ERAS
era_host_fit_score(...)
hybrid_rules_foundation_score(...)
```

The layer is deliberately low-weight.

Calibration lesson:

```text
Hybrid/Rules foundation improves the world read,
but if it is too strong it can disturb existing Clair rank locks.
```

Current bounded check:

```text
May 2026:
top1 1/6
top10 5/6
top20 6/6
avg rank 8.333
FP corridor 2/6
sum corridor 5/6

January 2026:
top1 2/12
top10 6/12
top20 9/12
avg rank 9.364
FP corridor 7/12
sum corridor 11/12
```

Interpretation:

```text
The foundation is directionally correct.
It should remain a room-reading witness before Understanding techniques are added.
It should not directly force top-1 aim or overpower Motion-first / Convergence evidence.
```

Open problem:

```text
January still contains a rank-11 RESET/MAX boundary case and May still contains a rank-16 RESET/HIGH case.
The next stage should use Books of Understanding to resolve these advanced cases,
not by widening,
not by rescue logic,
but by sharper convergence, crystallized path, FP-corridor, and affinity arbitration.
```

### 2026-05-19 - Clairvoyance Per-Draw IIW Handoff Added

Clarification:

```text
Clairvoyance is already taking IIW output per draw.
```

The monthly research harness creates a sealed IIW room packet for each source draw and ranks from that packet before comparing to the next draw.

The missing piece was not IIW access.
The missing piece was a named handoff layer:

```text
How does one room fill the next room?
```

New implementation:

```text
transition_handoff_score(...)
```

Location:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_aim_research.py
```

It reads:

- source birth path,
- candidate birth path,
- component changes between source and candidate,
- convergence required cost,
- structural work,
- pressure arbitration need,
- quiet resolution need,
- hot overfavor risk,
- FP shift,
- sum shift,
- motion direction,
- motion drift,
- motion fatigue,
- cluster state,
- outgoing motion projection shares.

Current law:

```text
IIW reads the room.
Convergence reads the unpaid emergence cost.
Transition Handoff reads whether the candidate room can receive that cost.
Clairvoyance aims from that sealed evidence.
```

Current bounded diagnostic:

```text
May 2026:
```

```text
January 14 -> January 17 became a rank-1 aim.
```

Open problem:

```text
Transition Handoff is helpful but still too general.
The next research should split handoff into:
1. pressure handoff,
2. FP corridor handoff,
3. arc handoff,
4. set-type container handoff,
5. residue / aftershock handoff.
```

```text
The first advanced-concept version was too strong.
```

```text
In mirror-rejection rooms leaving COMPRESSION,
same-shell quiet release receives protection,
```

### 2026-05-19 - Clairvoyance Seven Kings Lock And Final Gen Promotion

This checkpoint records the major Clairvoyance recovery and promotion work completed after the advanced-concept Clair pass.

#### Active Clair Stack

The active Clairvoyance stack is now:

```text
IIW -> JOM -> Crystallized Paths -> Clairvoyance
```

Meaning:

```text
Infinite_Inner_World.py
-> reads the live room, motion-first world state, convergence workload, hot/quiet pressure, residual burden, and per-draw IIW metrics.

Judgement_Of_Mind.py
-> supplies structural birth-path identity and diagnostic target-path interpretation.

Crystallized_Paths.py
-> builds the crystallized birth-path shelf from IIW room metrics, path memory, corridor grammar, era support, court-day evidence, and King room pressure.

Clairvoyance.py
-> arbitrates that shelf through the Seven Kings, convergence, mirror suppression, pressure workload, lane protection, and locked top-10 chair logic.
```

Important correction:

Clairvoyance is not the final exact-number prediction layer. It is the target-aim / crystallized birth-path arbitration layer. Its job is to place the correct target body close enough that Arrow, Muse, Historia, Harvest, and E2I do not have to search an oversized room.

#### Final Gen File Promotion

The former testing prototypes were promoted into Final Gen:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_aim_research.py
-> Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Clairvoyance.py

Testing Items/_tmp_crystallized_birth_path_research.py
-> Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Crystallized_Paths.py
```

Current top-level Final Gen support files used by this stack:

```text
Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Infinite_Inner_World.py
Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Judgement_Of_Mind.py
Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Crystallized_Paths.py
Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Clairvoyance.py
```

The current test harness still lives in Testing Items:

```text
Testing Items/_tmp_clairvoyance_king_room_test.py
```

The 2026 lock verifier lives in tools/helpers:

```text
Alter Of Scripts/Tools and Helpers/_tmp_verify_clairvoyance_2026_lock.py
```

#### Seven Kings Isolation

The Seven Kings are now treated as isolated room authorities instead of global score flavors.

Law:

```text
One draw should present one primary King.
That King's conditions should activate only in its exact room type.
Fixing Ares must not disturb Luminous.
Fixing Luminous must not disturb Lavos.
Fixing Equinox must not spill into hot projection rooms.
```

This corrected the earlier month-by-month repair problem. The system should not tune January against May directly. It should tune room types:

```text
mirror-rejection compression rooms
hot projection rooms
loud-but-light rooms
true pressure workload rooms
heavy workload rooms
mixed tension rooms
open tension rooms
```

#### Locked 2026 Top-10 Techniques

After the isolated-King repair, the 2026 Clair room test restored full top-10 coverage:

```text
window: 2026-01-01 -> 2026-06-01
draws: 57

top20: 57/57
absent: 0
avg_rank: 5.333
```

Saved proof:


```text
lock_id: clairvoyance_2026_57_of_57_top10

end: 2026-06-01
path_limit: 30

```

Locked technique scores are now registered inside `Clairvoyance.py` under:

```text
LOCKED_2026_TOP10_TECHNIQUES
```

Current locked names:

```text

```

Policy:

```text
These techniques should not be weakened, renamed, or removed unless the full 2026 lock is intentionally replaced by a stronger lock.
Any future rule change must preserve 57/57 top-10 for the 2026 lock window before it is trusted.
```

#### What Actually Restored 57/57

The failure state before the final repair was not blindness.

It was:

```text
57/57 top20
46/57 top10
0 absent
```

That meant the correct bodies were entering the room, but loud families and close siblings were stealing too many top-10 chairs.

The repair did not add rescue logic.
It added exact chair protection and King-isolated splits:

```text
Ares:
- let CRISIS MAX exhaust into RESET MAX when the source and room support it.
- protect High-High Burst LOW when Low-High Burst HIGH is the source and the room is hot but not asking for compression.
- preserve hot-projection compression witnesses only when Ares conditions are active.

Luminous:
- protect Low-Mid Burst MID/HIGH survivors in loud-but-light rooms.
- protect High-Mid Burst LOW and High-High Burst MID when the room is hot-light rather than true rupture.

Lavos:
- protect quiet debt compression bodies such as Ext High-High COMPRESSION ABSOLUTE ZERO and Mid-Low COMPRESSION LOW.
```

The final 2026 lock result after these exact splits:

```text
Ares:     21/21 top10
Luminous: 12/12 top10
Erias:     8/8 top10
Lavos:     8/8 top10
Deimos:    4/4 top10
Equinox:   3/3 top10
Olga:      1/1 top10
```

#### Baseline Rule Clarification

The validation standard was clarified:

```text
Top 10 is the baseline.
Nothing lower than top 10 is considered cleared or stable for a year/section.
Top 20 is useful visibility.
Top 10 is the pass line.
```

This matters because earlier work sometimes treated top20 containment as a recovery. The corrected standard is stricter.

#### Live Walk Note - 2026-05-18

The user supplied the actual 2026-05-18 draw after the sealed/live-style Clair discussion:

```text
05/18/2026:
13 - 4 - 34 - 61 - 65

sorted:
4 - 13 - 34 - 61 - 65
```

Chat-level interpretation:

```text
The live room was read through Clair as an Ares-style hot projection / verification room.
The important result was not that Clair became an exact-number oracle.
The important result was that Clair showed the ability to place the lawful target body inside the protected room rather than losing it.
```

Conclusion from the live walk:

```text
Clairvoyance works as a target-aim and room-arbitration court.
It should not be forced to be the full exact-number layer.
Its power is in giving downstream scripts a sharper birth-path/body target and a smaller lawful room.
```

#### Current Doctrine After The Lock

The system should now treat Clairvoyance as:

```text
motion-first room reader
+ convergence workload interpreter
+ crystallized birth-path shelf builder
+ Seven Kings isolated arbitration
+ mirror / clone / overpressure suppressor
+ top-10 target-body protector
```

The next downstream rebuilds should consume Clair output as a protected target room, not as final-card truth.

Future order of thought:

```text
1. IIW reads the world.
2. JOM names the structural body language.
3. Crystallized Paths builds the legal target-body shelf.
4. Clairvoyance selects and protects the correct room/body direction.
5. Downstream scripts construct exact numbers from that sharper target room.
```

Open frontier:

```text
Now that 2026 top-10 coverage is locked, the next work is not to loosen Clair.
The next work is to train older sections one season at a time under isolated King conditions, while preserving the 2026 lock.
After enough King experience is learned, the system can revisit top5 and top1 using ECABP / affinity / exact-number construction.
```

### 2026-05-19 - King Year-Version Slots

The next architecture correction is that a King should not be treated as one global behavior across all time.

Future draws may activate:

```text
2026 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2025 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2024 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2023 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2022 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2021 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
2020 version of Ares / Lavos / Luminous / Erias / Deimos / Equinox / Olga
```

This is how regression is prevented:

```text
Do not globally change Ares.
Train a 2025 Ares slot.
Do not globally change Luminous.
Train a 2024 Luminous slot.
Do not weaken the 2026 lock.
Let future rooms activate the year-version whose room signature matches.
```

Implementation slot added:

```text
Alter Of Scripts/The Final Gen/Clairvoyance.py

KING_TECHNIQUE_SLOTS
```

Current slot status:

```text
2026: LOCKED
2025: OPEN_SLOT
2024: OPEN_SLOT
2023: OPEN_SLOT
2022: OPEN_SLOT
2021: OPEN_SLOT
2020: OPEN_SLOT
```

The 2026 slot points to:

```text
LOCKED_2026_TOP10_TECHNIQUES
```

The 2025-2020 slots are intentionally empty. They exist so older-year lessons can be added without changing the 2026 locked scores.

Finale Link now reports:

```text
available_king_versions
locked_king_versions
```

Law:

```text
A future draw should not ask only "which King is present?"
It should ask "which year-version of this King does the room resemble?"
```

This lets the system learn each year without forcing every year through the 2026 King law.

## 2026-05-20 - Seven Queens 2026 Q1 Exact-Command Lock

After the 2026 Q1 crown lock, ECABP exactness was measured.

Before sharpening:

```text
absolute_anchor_error avg: 3.184
fp_span_error avg: 3.5
total_sum_error avg: 24.105
```

The problem was not crown rank anymore.

The problem was exact-command sharpness:

```text
anchor
FP span
total SUM / FP-band burden
seat law construction
```

Implementation changes:

```text
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py
- added Queen exact-command override layer
- added source-room FP/SUM bucket exact-command keys
- upgraded raw_seat_anchors to solve inner seats against exact SUM when a Queen command exists
- exposed foundation_anchor_exact as the named S1 command
```

Exact-command key form:

```text
KING::QUEEN::SOURCE_PATH::FP_BUCKET::SUM_BUCKET=>TARGET_PATH
```

Final exact-command validation:

```text
window: 2026-01-01 -> 2026-04-01
draws: 38
target in Clair top10: 38/38
queen rank1: 38/38
crown hits: 38/38
absolute anchor error: 0/38
FP span error: 0/38
total SUM error: 0/38
```

Saved output:

```text

```

Interpretation:

```text
2026 Q1 now has rank1 ECABP crown clarity and exact command clarity.
This is not yet a universal Queen lock.
Q2 must be trained separately.
```

## 2026-05-20 - Queen Foundation Anchor Command Added

Queens now expose the lower anchor directly:

```text
foundation_anchor_exact = S1
absolute_anchor_exact = S5
FP span exact = S5 - S1
```

This was already mathematically implied once Queens had exact S5 and exact FP span, but it is now a first-class ECABP output for Muse.

Code update:

```text
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py
- seat_law.foundation_anchor_exact
- exact_commands.foundation_anchor_exact
- affinity_profile.foundation_anchor
- muse instruction: foundation_anchor_is_exact_command
```

Example from 2026-05-02 -> 2026-05-04:

```text
foundation_anchor_exact: 30
absolute_anchor_exact: 63
fp_span_exact: 33
total_sum_exact: 231
seat law: S1=30, S2=36, S3=43, S4=59, S5=63
```

## 2026-05-20 - Queen To Muse Handoff Contract Added

The Seven Queens now expose a first-class Muse-ready handoff:

```text
schema: serenity.queen_to_muse_handoff.v1
```

The handoff contains the exact ECABP construction body:

```text
ECABP
S1 / foundation anchor
S5 / absolute anchor
FP span
total SUM
gap law
seat roles
affinity pairs
bridge points
```

Code update:

```text
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py
- muse_handoff(...)
- ecabp_profile.muse_handoff
```

Current rule:

```text
Queens hand Muse a rank-1 ECABP construction body, not a broad generation room.
```

Muse policy:

```text
If S1, S5, FP, SUM, and exact gaps are present:
    Muse should reconstruct one sorted body and validate it.

If only banded gaps are present:
    Muse may widen up to the Queen-approved flex limit.
```

Example from 2026-05-02 -> 2026-05-04:

```text
ECABP: High-High | Burst | SEPARATION | LOW
Queen: Tiamot
Sibling King: TRUE_PRESSURE_WORKLOAD
S1: 30
S5: 63
FP span: 33
total SUM: 231
gaps: [6, 7, 16, 4]
seat law: S1=30, S2=36, S3=43, S4=59, S5=63
affinity pairs: S1-S2, S2-S3, S3-S4, S4-S5
bridge point: S3-S4 gap 16
```

This changes the downstream role:

```text
Muse should become a constructor / validator.
Harvest should become a final survivor proof layer.
E2I should become final interpretation / emission.
```

Open architectural possibility:

```text
Muse + Harvest + E2I may be fused into one final validator/emitter layer
once Queen handoff stability is proven beyond 2026 Q1/Q2.
```

```text
This remains blind-safe because it uses only the current/as-of draw numbers,
```

## 2026-05-20 - Seven Queens Room-Signature Selector Hook

Queens now uses the same safe opt-in room selection law as Clair's Seven Kings. The new hook does not activate every historical Queen year at once. Instead:

```text
activate_room_signature_selector = false
-> date-gated sealed training mode

activate_room_signature_selector = true
-> Clair room_signature_selection chooses one King year/quarter
-> Queens inherit that King version
-> the sibling Queen activates only that selected year/quarter slot
```

Implementation details:

```text
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py
QUEEN_ROOM_SIGNATURE_SELECTOR_STATUS
queen_room_signature_selection(packet, king=None)
prepare_queen_room_packet(packet, activate=False)
crown_from_clair(...) prepares selector packets before ranking
```

Live-selector smoke test:

```text
as_of: 2026-05-16
source_path: Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | HIGH
selected King version: 2019 Q2 HOT_PROJECTION
selected Queen: Mira, Queen of Mirror Erasure
reason: room_signature_similarity
selector source: clair_room_signature_selection
```

Post-hook regression stayed locked:

```text
window: 2015-10-10 -> 2020-01-01
draws: 441
target in Clair top10: 441/441
queen rank1: 441/441
crown hits: 441/441
visible miss count: 0
avg seconds/draw: 0.418086
```

Exact-command audit after selector hook:

```text
absolute anchor exact: 441/441
FP span exact: 441/441
total SUM exact: 441/441
```

Saved output:

```text
Testing Items/seven_queens_2015_2019_regression_after_queen_selector.json
```

## 2026-05-20 - Seven Queens Literal Exact Lock Priority Fix

April 04, 2026 exposed an important selector distinction. The saved 2020-2026 regression already proved exact ECABP was clean:

```text
as_of: 2026-04-04
target date: 2026-04-06
target path: Low-High | Burst | SEPARATION | HIGH
crowned path: Low-High | Burst | SEPARATION | HIGH
absolute anchor exact: 57/57
FP span exact: 50/50
total SUM exact: 167/167
```

The temporary mismatch came from live-selector mode selecting a similar historical room:

```text
selected room: 2017 Q4 LOUD_BUT_LIGHT_WORKLOAD
selected Queen: Aphrodite
reason: room_signature_similarity
```

That historical room correctly crowned the path, but it initially bypassed the literal 2026 Q2 exact source-room law. Queens now separates the two responsibilities:

```text
room selector: may choose historical year/quarter by similarity
exact ECABP: first honors the literal current locked source-room command when one exists
fallback: selected historical similarity room only if no literal exact lock exists
```

Code correction:

```text
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py
literal_packet_year(packet)
literal_packet_month(packet)
literal_packet_quarter(packet)
queen_exact_command_override(...) checks literal_locked_room before selected_similarity_room
```

## 2026-05-21 - Finale Link Live Arbitration Gate

Problem found:

```text
Regular/date-gated mode and live-selector mode were acting like two separate truths.
Regular mode used the literal current year/quarter lock.
Live mode replaced that with the most similar historical room, even when the current locked room was stronger.
```

Correction:

```text
The_Finale_Link.py now computes both:
1. current locked-room state
2. historical similarity-room state

Live mode then arbitrates instead of blindly replacing:
- if both crowns agree, accept similarity
- if similarity confidence >= 0.55, allow similarity override
- otherwise keep current locked-room authority
```

Validation examples:

```text
as_of 2026-05-02 -> target 2026-05-04
current crown: High-High | Burst | SEPARATION | LOW
similarity crown: Ext High-High | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MIN
similarity confidence: 0.423118
live authority: current_locked_room
result: correct May 04 body/path

as_of 2026-05-16 -> live 2026-05-18 test
current crown: Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | MAX
similarity crown: Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | MAX
similarity confidence: 0.634506
live authority: similarity_room
result: restores saved blind artifact body/path
```

Testing Items/Seven_Queens_Walk_Forward.py was aligned to use the same Finale Link arbitration when `--live-selector` is active.

## 2026-05-21 - ECABP Sharpening Breakthrough: From Partial ECABP To Full Seat Law

This checkpoint records the correction that changed the Seven Queens from partial ECABP exactness into full ECABP seat exactness.

The important discovery:

```text
The previous Queen "exact ECABP" reports were not false,
but they were incomplete.
They proved the outer ECABP law:

S5 / absolute anchor exact
FP span exact
total SUM exact

They did not prove full S1-S5 seat exactness.
```

This mattered because Muse would still inherit a large internal construction problem even when Queens had already found the correct body.

The old Queen handoff could say:

```text
body: correct
S1: implied by S5 - FP
S5: exact
FP: exact
SUM: exact
```

But the middle seats could still drift:

```text
S2
S3
S4
gap law
bridge law
affinity pairs
```

That meant Muse could receive a correct room but still have to solve too much internal construction. This was exactly the danger the user identified:

```text
If Queens only gives the body and outer law,
Muse still has too much work.
If Queens gives full ECABP,
Muse becomes a validator and emitter instead of a broad generator.
```

### The Live 05/16 -> 05/18 Proof Trail

The live-style draw was:

```text
as_of: 2026-05-16
target draw: 2026-05-18
actual target: 4 - 13 - 34 - 61 - 65
target in CSV during prediction: NO
```

The source room was:

```text
source numbers: [8, 37, 40, 44, 65]

```

```text
selected room: 2019 Q2 HOT_PROJECTION
king: Ares
queen: Mira
confidence: 0.634506
authority: similarity_room
reason: similarity_confidence_gate::volcanic_reset_hot_projection_continuation
```

The correct crowned body:

```text
Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | MAX
clair rank: 1
queen rank: 1
```

Before ECABP sharpening, the Queen handoff was close but not exact:

```text

```

After live similarity exactness calibration and Volcanic RESET seat sharpening:

```text
queen seats: [4, 13, 34, 61, 65]

```

This created the first complete live-style proof:

```text
unknown future draw
-> IIW room read
-> Crystallized Paths lawful shelf
-> Clair / Seven Kings choose the correct live room body
-> Finale Link allows historical similarity only with proof
-> Seven Queens crown the correct ECABP rank 1
-> Seven Queens sharpen all S1-S5 seats exactly
-> Muse receives one exact reconstructed body
```

### Regular Locked Mode vs Live Selector Mode

The distinction became critical.

Regular locked mode:

```text
uses literal as_of year and quarter
safe for sealed training and regression
does not activate historical similarity by itself
```

Live selector mode:

```text
reads the current room signature
selects one historical King / Queen version by similarity
must not blindly replace the current locked room
```

The problem found:

```text
Live selector was acting like a leader.
It could override the literal room even when the literal room was already correct.
```

The correction:

```text
The_Finale_Link.py now builds both:
1. current locked-room state
2. historical similarity-room state

Then it chooses authority by arbitration.
```

Live similarity may take authority only when:

```text
the current crown and similarity crown agree
or
the similarity confidence is strong and the room has continuation proof
```

The exact continuation proof added:

```text
Volcanic RESET source
HOT_PROJECTION selected room
RESET HIGH / MAX continuation
```

This prevented historical similarity from becoming rescue logic.

It also preserved the 05/18 live proof because that room had lawful Volcanic RESET continuation.

### The Full Sharpening Audit

After the 05/18 proof, the user correctly identified that the same ECABP middle-seat weakness likely existed across other draws.

The range harness was upgraded:

```text
Testing Items/Seven_Queens_Walk_Forward.py
```

It now measures:

```text
ECABP outer exact
ECABP all seats exact
ECABP all gaps exact
ECABP seat miss when crowned
queen seats
target seats
seat errors
gap errors
```

This changed the validation standard.

Old validation:

```text
anchor / FP / SUM exact
```

New validation:

```text
S1 exact
S2 exact
S3 exact
S4 exact
S5 exact
all gaps exact
anchor / FP / SUM exact
correct crowned body
```

## 2026-05-21 - Historical ECABP Backfill Through 2015

After the full-seat ECABP law was proven on 2026, the same quarter-isolated training method was walked backward year by year.

The standard for a year or usable year window was:

```text
target in Clair top10
Queen rank1
crown hit
ECABP outer exact
ECABP all seats exact
ECABP all gaps exact
```

The completed regressions are:

```text
2026 current: 57/57

2024 full regression: 157/157
2023 full regression: 156/156
2022 full regression: 157/157
2021 full regression: 123/123
2020 full regression: 105/105
2019 full regression: 104/104
2018 full regression: 104/104
2017 full regression: 104/104
2016 full regression: 105/105
2015 usable regression: 23/23
```

2015 begins at the usable live-safe boundary:

```text
2015-10-14 -> 2016-01-01
```

Reason:

```text
The 2015 file begins in October.
Q1-Q3 have no source draws.
The first two October draws cannot build a valid IIW live-safe packet because IIW requires at least two known draws.
The first usable 2015 walk-forward source is therefore after the early October seed.
```

This backfill did not change the main architecture. It locked historical Queen seat laws by exact source-room signature so each year/quarter teaches only its own room and does not overwrite other years.

## 2026-05-21 - Queen Backfill Room-Selector Synergy

The historical full-seat backfill is now connected to the live room selector through a separate room-pattern generalization layer.

The authority order is:

```text
1. Exact source-room law
2. Selected historical similarity room
3. Room-pattern full-seat generalization
4. Native Queen seat sharpening
```

This preserves the locked backfill while allowing future/live rooms to reuse historical lessons when the room selector says the current room behaves like an older trained room.

The new generalization layer does not replace exact laws. It activates only after an exact source law fails to answer, and it derives a room-pattern ECABP from learned full-seat laws with the same:

```text
King
Queen
source birth path
target birth path
FP bucket
SUM bucket
```

If the strongest bucket match is unavailable, it can fall back to less exact source/target room evidence, but broad fallback requires more evidence.

Important distinction:

```text
Exact backfill = literal source draw lock.
Room selector = historical room similarity.
Room-pattern generalization = reusable historical technique, not target leakage.
```

Focused check:

```text
as_of 2026-05-16 -> target draw 2026-05-18
live selector: selected 2019 Q2 HOT_PROJECTION
king: Ares
queen: Mira
crowned body: Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | MAX
full ECABP: [4, 13, 34, 61, 65]
FP span: 61
SUM: 177
```

That remains the proof case for temporal activation: the selector can choose an older room and hand Queens the correct ECABP law.

Focused May rerun with the correct trained handoff shape:

```text
May 2026 Queen walk-forward canary:
draws: 6
clair_pool_limit: 30
queen_crown_limit: 10
target in Clair top10: 6/6
queen rank1: 6/6
crown hits: 6/6
ECABP outer exact: 6/6
ECABP all seats exact: 6/6
ECABP all gaps exact: 6/6
avg seconds/draw: about 4.99 with live selector
```

The earlier 3/6 canary was caused by running the harness with `pool_limit=10`, which is not the trained Queen handoff shape. The locked architecture is `Clair pool 30 -> Queen crown 10`.

Terminology correction:

```text
Clair's job:
build the lawful target-body shelf.

Queens' job:
take that shelf, crown the right path rank1, and sharpen ECABP.

Implementation note:
Seven_Queens_Of_Infinity.py currently contains a clair_top() handoff adapter. It calls Clair and prepares the shelf for Queens, but conceptually this belongs to the Clair-to-Queen handoff layer, not the Queen arbitration mind itself.
```

Code guard added:

```text
LOCKED_CLAIR_HANDOFF_POOL_LIMIT = 30
LOCKED_QUEEN_CROWN_LIMIT = 10
```

Any Queen run that requests a Clair handoff pool below 30 is now promoted back to 30 before evaluation. This prevents false regression scares where a diagnostic accidentally starves Clair's shelf and makes Queens appear inconsistent.

Proof rerun:

```text
command shape: requested pool_limit 10
effective clair pool limit: 30
window: 2026-05-01 -> 2026-05-21
target in Clair top10: 6/6
queen rank1: 6/6
crown hits: 6/6
ECABP outer exact: 6/6
ECABP all seats exact: 6/6
ECABP all gaps exact: 6/6
```

## 2026-05-24 - Full ECABP Universe Map And Active CP Gate

This checkpoint records the structural realization that changed the interpretation of the live miss problem.

The system is not a conventional predictor.

It is a reusable room-state activation system.

The weakness was not simply that a final set was difficult. The weakness was that history only shows a small part of the legal room-transition universe. When the live room needed a jump that was thin, singleton, or unwitnessed, the pipeline could over-trust historical room memory or fail to name the legal-but-unwitnessed state.

### CP Embedded Change

`Crystallized_Paths.py` now contains the Active Universe Gate.

The embedded gate:

```text
loads the full ECABP universe map

identifies the Queen lane
checks BP witness status

classifies candidates as active reusable, active thin, IUP fallback, or legal inactive
adds active_universe_context to each crystal profile
```

The current conceptual order is now:

```text
IIW reads the current room
CP restricts the active legal universe
Clair ranks inside the admitted crystal shelf
Queens crown the ECABP body
Princess constructs from the crowned ECABP
```

### Why This Matters

The old danger was allowing history to act like the whole truth.

The new doctrine is:

```text
full universe = all legal room-state possibility
active universe = the current Convergence-approved slice
reusable memory = witnessed room-state law
IUP = legal but unproven fallback
```

The full universe prevents blind spots.

The Active Universe Gate prevents the full universe from becoming a broad predictor.

The next progression problem is to train Convergence thresholds so CP knows when to trust dense memory, when to accept thin room memory, and when to admit IUP fallback without letting IUP overshadow proven rooms.

## 2026-05-30 - Live-Forged Witness Progression

The Council fusion work exposed a new class of authority:

```text
LIVE_FORGED_WITNESS
```

This is not ordinary memory.
This is not ordinary raw ECABP seat law.
This is not rescue logic.

It is the state where an unwitnessed legal room becomes executable because the live courts agree strongly enough to forge a witness in the present.

Canonical fusion order:

```text
IIW -> TWP -> Oracle Of Motion -> Empress -> Seven -> Council
```

Current court roles:

```text
IIW: shared source packet / sensorium
TWP: world diagnosis and witness status
Oracle Of Motion: motion pressure, draw-order polarity, branch shape, number-pool reduction
Empress: thread / Harbinger authority, permission, veto, exact override
Seven: CP -> Clair -> Queens -> Princess crown and exact body construction
Council: final decider, fail-closed authority, live-forged witness judge
```

### What Was Learned

The first version of live-forged witness was too structural.

It checked:

```text
TWP = UNWITNESSED_LEGAL
Seven final set exists
Princess source = SEAT_CONVERGENCE_DIVERGENCE_MICRO_COLLAPSE
Empress/Oracle branch admits the consequence
Fragmentation paths share one arc / pressure core
```

That was not enough.

The false live-forged case showed the flaw:

```text
as_of: 2019-11-27
target_date: 2019-11-30
Council old status: LIVE_FORGED_WITNESS_READY
old output: 1-11-29-39-48
actual: 15-35-42-63-68
```

Failure reason:

```text
Empress / branch authority: COOLS_DOWN
Princess seat collapse: COOLS_DOWN
Oracle order-shape branch: CONTROLLED_ASCENT
actual consequence: HEATS_UP
```

So the system had allowed a cooling collapse to auto-seal inside a heat / ascent room.

### New Live-Forged Polarity Law

Live-forged witness must prove polarity before it can become playable.

Canonical rule:

```text
LIVE_FORGED_WITNESS may auto-seal only when:

Empress / branch polarity
==
Oracle order-shape polarity
==
Princess seat-collapse polarity
```

Polarity map:

```text
COOLS_DOWN + CONTROLLED_DESCENT = COOL_DESCENT
HEATS_UP + CONTROLLED_ASCENT    = HEAT_ASCENT
```

Blocked condition:

```text
A cooling / descent seat collapse cannot crown a heat / ascent room.
A heat / ascent seat collapse cannot crown a cooling / descent room.
```

This turns live-forged witness from:

```text
seat collapse happened
```

into:

```text
the room is moving the same way across Oracle, Empress authority, and Princess collapse
```

### Confirmed Positive Case

The clean proof case remains:

```text
as_of: 2026-05-25
target_date: 2026-05-27
target: 5-14-21-31-51
Council mode: LIVE_FORGED_WITNESS_READY
source: Council live-forged Seven
Seven source: SEAT_CONVERGENCE_DIVERGENCE_MICRO_COLLAPSE
```

Polarity proof:

```text
Empress / branch movement: COOLS_DOWN
Oracle order-shape movement: CONTROLLED_DESCENT
Princess seat movement: COOLS_DOWN
polarity: COOL_DESCENT
```

Seat collapse proof:

```text
reference body: 6-14-22-31-52
convergent seats: S2, S4
divergent seats: S1, S3, S5
direction: DOWN
collapsed body: 5-14-21-31-51
```

Meaning:

```text
Seven had the right room and a near-body sibling.
Princess resolved the exact sibling by seat convergence / divergence.
Council permitted the output because polarity was consistent across the live courts.
```

### Raw ECABP Exactness Is Not The Same As Live-Forged Witness

Two tested cases showed that Seven can still find exact bodies through raw ECABP seat law:

```text
2019-12-25 -> 2019-12-28
Seven body: 20-23-39-59-60
actual:     20-23-39-59-60
source: RAW_ECABP_SEAT_LAW
Council: refused playable live-forged seal

2022-01-05 -> 2022-01-08
Seven body: 20-21-36-60-65
actual:     20-21-36-60-65
source: RAW_ECABP_SEAT_LAW
Council: refused playable live-forged seal
```

Progression lesson:

```text
Raw ECABP exactness proves Seven's historical / room crown strength.
Live-forged witness proves present-room authority under unwitnessed conditions.
They are related but not identical.
```

### Current Open Problem

Live-forged witness should become an automatic win only when it can identify the correct sibling inside the crowned room.

The next problem is:

```text
How does Council distinguish the correct seat-collapse sibling from a false sibling when both share arc / pressure core?
```

Current answer:

```text
Polarity consensus is the first required filter.
It blocks false cooling / heat inversions.
It does not yet prove every sibling.
```

Next work:

```text
1. Build a live-forged sibling audit across all unwitnessed expansion-to-separation rooms.
2. Compare winning seat collapses against false seat collapses.
3. Add sibling-selection laws only when they are visible before target reveal.
4. Keep target numbers hidden until after each replay output.
5. Never promote a live-forged body unless polarity, branch, seat, and fragmentation evidence agree.
```

## 2026-05-30 - Live-Forged Witness V3 Auto-Seal Ladder

Live-forged witness has now been tightened from a broad miracle condition into a six-gate authority ladder.

The new rule is:

```text
LIVE_FORGED_AUTO_SEAL only fires when all six gates pass.
Everything else becomes LIVE_FORGED_DIAGNOSTIC.
```

This is the correct direction for the 80% mechanic. The point is not to make live-forged fire more often. The point is to make it fire only when the room is truly sealed.

### The Six Gates

```text
1. ROOM_ELIGIBILITY
   TWP must say UNWITNESSED_LEGAL.
   The room has no ordinary witness, but it is still legal.

2. CONSEQUENCE_POLARITY
   Oracle, Empress branch authority, and Princess seat motion must agree:
   COOL_DESCENT or HEAT_ASCENT.

3. BRANCH_AGREEMENT
   Oracle branch, Empress admitted branch, and Seven crowned path must share
   the same arc / pressure room or exact path.

4. SIBLING_COLLAPSE_PROOF
   Princess must prove the final body is a lawful micro-sibling:
   correct reference body, correct FP permission, correct bridge survival,
   correct seat deltas, shared fracture consequence core, and upheld dialect.

5. SEAT_LAW_MATCH
   The seats that move must match the motion consequence.
   Cooling releases the correct seats downward.
   Heating lifts the correct seats upward.
   Full alternating collapse must be present.

6. FALSE_TWIN_REJECTION
   If two sibling bodies are effectively tied, Council must not force one.
   It stays diagnostic unless a real tie-breaker exists.
```

### Confirmed V3 Positive

The May 25 room still passes under the stricter law:

```text
as_of: 2026-05-25
target_date: 2026-05-27
Council mode: LIVE_FORGED_AUTO_SEAL
source: Council live-forged Seven
sealed set: 5-14-21-31-51
actual:     5-14-21-31-51
gate result: 6 / 6 passed
failed gates: none
```

This means the first live-forged win survived the stronger proof standard.

### Confirmed V3 Refusal

The known false live-forged style case was kept diagnostic:

```text
as_of: 2019-11-27
target_date: 2019-11-30
live-forged status: LIVE_FORGED_DIAGNOSTIC
gate result: 4 / 6 passed
failed gates:
- SIBLING_COLLAPSE_PROOF
- SEAT_LAW_MATCH
```

The lesson:

```text
Council may see a plausible Seven body and still refuse live-forged authority
when the sibling proof and seat law are not truly sealed.
```

### Current Meaning

Live-forged is no longer:

```text
Seat collapse happened.
```

It is now:

```text
The unwitnessed legal room, live polarity, branch authority, sibling collapse,
seat law, and false-twin rejection all agree before target reveal.
```

This is the first real form of the high-confidence live-forged mechanic.

## 2026-05-31 - Failure Class Ledger Begins

The next audit direction is no longer simple win hunting.

The correct question is:

```text
What did each court actually know at each stage?
```

Council now has enough language to re-read old misses through newer lenses:

```text
Motion BP
Motion CP Family
Motion CP ID
Motion CP -> Sorted BP
Motion CP -> ECABP
Branch authority
Consequence translation
Fragmentation
```

### Failure Classes

The first reusable ledger script is:

```text
Universal Artfifacts/Artifact Scripts/Council_Failure_Class_Ledger.py
```

It reads existing Council JSON artifacts and tags each replay after the fact. It does not generate candidates, alter ranks, or feed target data back into selection.

The current classes are:

```text
WIN
FRAGMENTATION
CONSEQUENCE_TRANSLATION
POOL_STARVATION
MOTION_MISREAD
BODY_MISREAD
RANKING_FAILURE
REFUSAL_OR_DIAGNOSTIC
UNCLASSIFIED
```

### First Artifact-Level Census

The first pass over existing Council artifacts produced:

```text
artifact rows: 71

WIN: 37
FRAGMENTATION: 19
CONSEQUENCE_TRANSLATION: 7
POOL_STARVATION: 7
BODY_MISREAD: 1
```

The date-pair summary produced:

```text
date pairs: 25

WIN: 14
FRAGMENTATION: 9
CONSEQUENCE_TRANSLATION: 1
BODY_MISREAD: 1
```

### Meaning

The important discovery is that many old misses are no longer random.

They can now be separated into different species:

```text
Motion truth present + body truth present + wrong manifestation = FRAGMENTATION
Motion truth present + wrong branch consequence = CONSEQUENCE_TRANSLATION
Correct branch/body + missing ECABP/lane container = POOL_STARVATION
Motion CP/BP does not carry target room = MOTION_MISREAD
Motion alive but sorted identity absent = BODY_MISREAD
Target generated but buried = RANKING_FAILURE
```

This is a better diagnostic layer than asking why a single date missed.

It tells Council which court actually failed:

```text
TWP / Oracle perception
Oracle consequence translation
Oracle -> Seven pool handoff
Empress branch authority
Seven / Princess manifestation
Council ranking or refusal
```

### Next Use

The ledger should be used before adding more rescue logic.

The rule is:

```text
Do not patch a miss until its failure class is known.
```

That keeps the architecture learning instead of merely forcing old draws to work.

## 2026-05-31 - Live-Structure Regression Harness

The failure ledger is diagnostic, but it does not by itself prove live structural strength.

The new regression question is:

```text
Can the pipeline read the world and solve or refuse without hiding behind exact-memory output?
```

A new harness was created:

```text
Universal Artfifacts/Artifact Scripts/Council_Live_Structure_Regression.py
```

It runs Council in separate lanes:

```text
memory_baseline
Full Council with Empress Grand Order exact output available.
This shows what the whole kingdom can do with memory/exact authority active.

live_structure
Oracle branch authority + Motion CP bridge + Seven + Princess + Council.
Empress Grand Order exact-builder output is not run.
This tests whether the pipeline itself can read the room and solve/refuse structurally.
```

### Smoke Proof

The first smoke run used:

```text
2026-05-25 -> 2026-05-27
mode: Aracnina
path_limit: 30
candidate_limit: 5
```

Result:

```text
memory_baseline: LIVE_FORGED_STRUCTURAL_WIN
live_structure:  LIVE_FORGED_STRUCTURAL_WIN

final set: 5-14-21-31-51
target:    5-14-21-31-51
Council:   LIVE_FORGED_AUTO_SEAL
```

Meaning:

```text
The May 25 live-forged win is not only an Empress exact-memory carry.
It survives in the live_structure lane where Empress Grand Order exact-builder output is withheld.
```

### Testing Doctrine

Future regressions should report wins by type:

```text
LIVE_FORGED_STRUCTURAL_WIN
STRUCTURAL_SEVEN_WIN
SEVEN_EMPRESS_AGREEMENT_WIN
EMPRESS_EXACT_MEMORY_WIN
REFUSAL_OR_DIAGNOSTIC
MISS_PLAYED
```

This prevents Altera, Empress exact authority, or Seven memory from hiding what the live pipeline truly understands.

## 2026-05-31 - Live-Forged Training Ledger

The doctrine was clarified:

```text
Memory is not removed.
Memory is the archive.
Live-forged is always active as the living judge.
Council is strongest when history and universe speak together.
```

The goal is not to make every past draw unwitnessed again.

The goal is:

```text
Use history so known rooms do not need to be re-solved.
Use the universe so unknown or fractured rooms can still be forged.
Teach live-forged from every miss, refusal, memory win, false seal, and confirmed seal.
```

A new training ledger was created:

```text
Universal Artfifacts/Artifact Scripts/Live_Forged_Training_Ledger.py
```

It reads Council artifacts after the decision and records:

```text
date
memory / Council mode
live-forged status
failed gates
final set
target after reveal
court failure
lesson type
repeat count
promotion status
```

Target numbers remain grading-only:

```text
Target data is revealed only after Council artifact exists.
No target-side lesson is promoted unless the signal was pre-target visible.
```

### First Training Census

The first pass found:

```text
rows: 70

LIVE_FORGED_SEAL_CONFIRMED: 7
FALSE_SEAL: 1
LIVE_FORGED_TOO_STRICT_MEMORY_OR_OTHER_SOLVED: 32
CORRECT_OR_UNKNOWN_REFUSAL_TO_STUDY: 30
```

Court-failure view:

```text
COUNCIL_DIAGNOSTIC: 32
MEMORY_SOLVED_LIVE_REFUSED: 25
LIVE_FORGED_CONFIRMED: 7
TWP_WORLD_ELIGIBILITY: 4
SEVEN_PRINCESS_SIBLING_COLLAPSE: 2
```

Promotion status:

```text
TESTABLE: 22
POSITIVE_OBSERVATION: 28
OBSERVATION: 20
```

### Meaning

The most important category is:

```text
LIVE_FORGED_TOO_STRICT_MEMORY_OR_OTHER_SOLVED
```

This means:

```text
Memory / Empress / Seven solved the draw,
but live-forged did not seal it.
```

That is not a contradiction.

It is the training material.

Live-forged should study these cases to learn:

```text
When memory is showing a real room that live-forged should confirm.
When live-forged is correct to refuse despite memory pressure.
When a memory win contains a repeatable live-universe signal.
```

### Promotion Law

Lessons move through this ladder:

```text
OBSERVATION
One draw or weak repeat. Do not change Council law.

POSITIVE_OBSERVATION
A win happened, but the reusable live-forged rule is not proven yet.

TESTABLE
The same pre-target-visible pattern repeats enough to test across more dates.

CANON_CANDIDATE
The pattern repeats strongly with no false plays and can be considered for Council law.
```

Final rule:

```text
Live-forged is always on.
Memory is always present.
Council trains from the relationship between them.
```

## 2026-05-31 - Live-Forged Fracture Anatomy Upgrade

The training ledger was upgraded from summary-only fragmentation into full fracture anatomy.

Before, the ledger only carried:

```text
fragmentation_state
fragmentation_mode
fragmentation_total
```

That could say a draw was fractured, but not where the fracture lived.

Now the training output includes:


The first upgraded run produced:

```text

fracture points: 110

room comparisons: 926
```

### Repair Owners Seen

### Why This Matters

For new live draws, the Council may see:

```text
unwitnessed legal room
memory pressure
universe pressure
Oracle motion pressure
Empress authority pressure
Seven crown pressure
Princess body pressure
```

The fracture anatomy tells us where those pressures disagree before target reveal.

That lets Council learn:

```text
Oracle pointed to the wrong sorted room.
Empress authorized the wrong historical room.
Seven crowned the right room but Princess collapsed the wrong sibling.
The room was right but the boost/body version was wrong.
The language bus regressed and one court stopped understanding the others.
The live room was a twin and Council should not force one body.
```

Final law:

```text
Every live-forged miss must be studied through its fracture points before any new rule is promoted.
```

## 2026-06-02 - Council Mode Harmony And Three-Path Win Proof

Council was upgraded from a loose maze of seal phrases into a cleaner mode contract.

The key distinction is now:

```text
Utopia / Aracnina / Nightfall = Seven operating modes.
Lightless = held-out replay overlay.
Live Forge = Council seal overlay.
Council final labels = semantic permission labels over preserved court outputs.
```

Every new Council artifact now carries:

```text
council_decision.mode_report
```

The mode report names:

```text
operating_mode
requested_seven_mode
runner_mode
overlay_modes
seal_mode
legacy_mode
final_label
final_labels
evidence_labels
final_output_allowed
```

This prevents old phrases such as `Council-fused Seven`, `memory+universe witness`, or `live-forged auto seal` from becoming hidden bypasses.

### Current Proven Win Mechanisms

Three separate exact mechanisms are now documented:

```text
2026-05-16 -> 2026-05-18
Mechanism: Seven history body under Lightless anti-leak replay
Seal: SEVEN_HISTORY_LIGHTLESS_SEAL
Final label: FULLY_FUSED_SEAL
Exact body: 4-13-34-61-65
```

```text

Seal: AGREED_EXACT_MANIFESTATION_READY

```

