```text
Seal: LIVE_FORGED_AUTO_SEAL
Final label: FULLY_FUSED_SEAL
Exact body: 5-14-21-31-51
```

### New Council Fix

The 2026-05-16 -> 2026-05-18 Lightless replay exposed a Council error.

Before the fix, Council called the exact Seven body `branch-fit alone` and preserved it only as diagnostic, even though the pre-result contract had:

```text
Lightless target-date mask active
TWP thin witness
Seven Queen/Princess exact body
Empress branch admission
Oracle clean contracts
Seven branch gate passed
Fragmentation SINGLE
No hard blockers
```

Council now recognizes this as:

```text
SEVEN_HISTORY_LIGHTLESS_SEAL
```

This seal is narrow. It only fires when Lightless prevents target-date leakage and the independent court contract is clean.

### Current Interpretation

The system is no longer showing one isolated win path.

It has now shown:

```text
pure history can win
history plus universe can win
unwitnessed legal Live Forge can win
```

The open problem is no longer whether the courts can ever produce exact bodies.

The open problem is:

```text
Which mode owns which situation before the draw?
```

The next progression work is mode routing:

```text
Use Lightless + Utopia for live-like replay acceptance.
Use Lightless + Aracnina for no-memory universe proof.
Use Utopia for normal guarded live operation.
Use Aracnina to test whether memory is secretly carrying the room.
Use Nightfall only for similarity stress diagnosis.
Use Live Forge only when the full witness ladder passes.
```

## 2026-06-03 - Playable Set Policy, Miss Taxonomy, And Second Lens Reality Check

The June 3 work changed the Council boundary and clarified what the current Lightless evidence is actually saying.

### Council Single-Set Playable Policy

Council was corrected so that a single court-produced body is no longer trapped as a diagnostic-only result.

Current law:

```text
When Council has one court-produced body, live operation emits it as the playable set.
Agreement, conflict, and diagnostic labels remain advisory evidence.
They cannot suppress the only body.
```

New Council label:

```text
PLAYABLE_SET_SEAL
```

Meaning:

- the system has one body to output
- the body is emitted as `recommended_output_set`
- old blockers are preserved as advisory evidence
- the label does not pretend every court fully agreed

`FULLY_FUSED_SEAL` is now reserved for cleaner full agreement. `PLAYABLE_SET_SEAL` is the live-facing one-body policy.

Smoke verification:

```text
Test: 2026-05-04 -> 2026-05-06
Mode: Lightless Utopia
Council mode: PLAYABLE_SET_SEAL
Legacy mode: THIN_ROOM_DIAGNOSTIC
Recommended set: 18-27-51-65-68
Diagnostic set: none
Policy status: PROMOTED_SINGLE_BODY_TO_PLAYABLE
```

### 2026 Lightless Utopia Combined Sweep

Current combined Lightless Utopia index:

```text
Testing Items/Fusion Council/Lightless Utopia 2026 Combined Sweep/LIGHTLESS_UTOPIA_2026_COMBINED_SWEEP_INDEX.json
```

Current sweep summary:

```text
Total tested windows: 62
Exact bodies: 43
Misses: 19
5/5: 43
1/5: 8
0/5: 11
2/5, 3/5, 4/5: 0
```

This means the current Lightless Utopia body behavior is split between exact collapse and low-overlap miss, not a smooth middle distribution.

### The 19 Misses - Current Taxonomy

The 19 misses are not all the same type of failure.

Near-body count:

```text
18/19 had at least one number within 5 of the actual body.
13/19 were strong near-body by the practical repair rule:
  3+ near lanes, or 1 exact hit plus 2+ near lanes.
2/19 had all five candidate numbers within 5 of the actual body.
```

Wrong-body count:

```text
11/19 had zero exact overlap.
5/19 were severe wrong-body cases: 0/5 exact and fewer than 3 near lanes.
0/19 were totally dead: 0/5 exact and no near lanes.
```

Authority failures:

```text
19/19 had some authority failure under old Council rules.
18/19 carried Empress authority refusal.
9/19 carried TWP-not-strong-enough.
7/19 carried Seven rejected by TWP world-fit or Empress authority.
```

Fragmentation failures:

```text
18/19 carried Fragmentation Resolver failure.
```

Motion translation failures:

```text
18/19 carried Oracle shared metric / motion translation incompleteness.
1/19 had Oracle metrics upheld: 2026-05-18 -> 2026-05-20.
```

Hard-room failures:

```text
10/19 were broad hard-room cases:
  THIN_STRICT_WITNESSED, UNWITNESSED_LEGAL, or SIMPLE_REUSABLE_ROOM.
7/19 had strict witnesses <= 1.
2/19 had strict witnesses = 0.
```

Current interpretation:

```text
Most misses were not random dead bodies.
Most misses were near-body or authority/translation/fragmentation-conflicted bodies.
The repair work should not start by rebuilding Seven.
The repair work should classify each miss by failure family, then decide whether the fix belongs to Oracle motion translation, Empress authority handoff, Seven collapse, Fragmentation Resolver, or Council routing.
```

### Second Lens Overlay A/B Check

The second lens overlay is wired into Clair and Queens, but it is not yet steering the crown.

Current code behavior:

```text
Clair can attach living_room_overlay.
Queens can attach living_room_overlay.
Princess can read motion_conditioned_room_notes.
```

Current test finding:

```text
May 4 -> May 6:
  with second lens: 18-27-51-65-68
  without second lens: 18-27-51-65-68
  crowned path unchanged
  Queen unchanged

May 18 -> May 20:
  with second lens: same crowned path, Queen, Princess, ECABP
  without second lens: same crowned path, Queen, Princess, ECABP
```

Conclusion:

```text
Second lens is currently an observation layer, not a steering layer.
It can describe the living room.
It does not yet rerank Clair, move Queens, or alter Princess collapse.
```

Next required second-lens work:

```text
Make second lens vote through measurable fields:
draw_order_signature
motion_cp_id
motion_bp
lane_pressure
direction/drift
motion_boundary
flow-to-outcome tendencies
oracle survival evidence
```

Until this is implemented, second lens should be treated as explanation and evidence, not as proven prediction force.

### Why Exact Wins Can Exist Without Target Draw Memory

Lightless blocks the held-out target court room and target-date exact solution shortcuts. Exact wins under Lightless therefore come from structural replay rather than direct target-copying.

Current explanation:

```text
IIW gives the source draw body and motion state.
TWP reads witness strength and room condition.
Oracle describes motion pressure and possible flow.
Empress judges authority and room permission from prior memory.
Seven collapses through Clair, Queens, ECABP, and Princess proof.
Council preserves the single body.
```

The exact-body path is:

```text
current draw condition -> motion/world witness -> similar historical room -> Seven collapse body -> Council output
```

This means the confirmed exact runs are not proof that every draw is solvable. They are proof that the current architecture can sometimes identify a lawful exact body from source-state structure without the target draw being available to the court.

### Next Work

Return to the 19 misses and display them in the active repair format:

```text
near-body
wrong body
authority failure
fragmentation failure
motion translation failure
hard-room failure
```

Then fix each miss family one at a time instead of applying broad changes across the whole system.

## 2026-06-03 - Miss Repair Phase 1 And Phase 2 Installed

Council now emits two replay-diagnostic repair packets after a body is selected.

These packets do not move a live set. They only grade the chosen body after target reveal so the system can learn the miss family without leaking target data into selection.

### Phase 1 - Full-Near Offset Corrector

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.full_near_offset_corrector
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.full_near_offset_corrector
```

It separates two full-near cases:

```text
FULL_SAME_SEAT_OFFSET_CORRECTION_AVAILABLE
All five sorted seats are within +/-5 and can be replay-corrected seat-by-seat.

FULL_NEAR_TRAIT_OFFSET_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
All five candidate numbers are near the target body, but target coverage fragments.
This means the room found the neighborhood, but one or more target numbers were double-claimed or missed.
```

Validation examples:

```text
2026-05-18 -> 2026-05-20
candidate: 14-24-35-47-61
actual:    10-28-30-46-57
status: FULL_SAME_SEAT_OFFSET_CORRECTION_AVAILABLE
deltas: -4, +4, -5, -1, -4
replay correction: exact
```

```text
2026-04-13 -> 2026-04-15
candidate: 10-16-24-30-40
actual:    13-21-27-43-45
status: FULL_NEAR_TRAIT_OFFSET_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
same-seat deltas: +3, +5, +3, +13, +5
finding: near neighborhood present, but coverage fragmented
missing target: 45
duplicate claim: 13
```

### Phase 2 - Lane Survival And Replacement Plan

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.lane_survival_replacement_plan
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.lane_survival_replacement_plan
```

It classifies each lane after replay grading:

```text
LOCK_SURVIVED_LANE
DRIFT_CORRECT_SAME_SEAT
REASSIGN_NEAR_TRAIT
REPLACE_DEAD_LANE
```

Main statuses:

```text
EXACT_BODY_ALL_LANES_SURVIVED
ONE_HIT_NEAR_BODY_DRIFT
FULL_NEAR_OFFSET_BODY
ZERO_HIT_NEAR_BODY_DRIFT
WRONG_BODY_OR_ROOM
PARTIAL_LANE_DRIFT
LIVE_NO_TARGET_AVAILABLE
NO_CANDIDATE_BODY
```

Validation examples:

```text
2026-02-21 -> 2026-02-23
status: ONE_HIT_NEAR_BODY_DRIFT
repair family: LANE_SURVIVAL_PLUS_REPLACEMENT
meaning: one lane survived, several lanes were near, final lane needed replacement.
```

```text
2026-05-18 -> 2026-05-20
status: FULL_NEAR_OFFSET_BODY
repair family: OFFSET_CORRECTION
meaning: the whole body was close, but shifted.
```

### Current Meaning

The first two miss-repair phases are now diagnostic infrastructure.

They let Council say:

```text
This miss was an offset body.
This miss was a near trait body with fragmented coverage.
This miss kept some lanes alive but needed replacement.
This miss was a wrong body or hard room.
```

The next required step is live-safe learning:

```text
Train historical offset and lane-survival profiles before target reveal.
Let Oracle motion decide when an offset profile or lane replacement profile is active.
Only then allow Phase 1 or Phase 2 evidence to influence live selection.
```

## 2026-06-03 - Miss Repair Phase 3 And Phase 4 Installed

Council now carries the next two diagnostic repair packets.

These are still intelligence layers, not live rescue logic.

### Phase 3 - Motion Neighborhood Arbitration

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.motion_neighborhood_arbitration
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.motion_neighborhood_arbitration
```

This phase handles the miss family where exact overlap is zero, but the candidate body is still close enough to prove the system found the nearby motion neighborhood.

Primary status:

```text
STRONG_MOTION_NEIGHBORHOOD_WRONG_COLLAPSE
```

Meaning:

```text
The room/motion family was probably nearby,
but Oracle/Seven/Princess collapsed the wrong sibling body.
```

It records:

```text
candidate body
target body after replay reveal
near lanes
dead lanes
candidate gaps
target gaps
gap deltas
sum delta
front / middle / tail drift
Oracle motion context
Motion CP -> ECABP bridge status
```

Live-safe next step:

```text
Train Oracle to choose between nearby motion siblings before Seven/Princess collapse.
```

### Phase 4 - Room Disagreement Arbitration

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.room_disagreement_arbitration
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.room_disagreement_arbitration
```

This phase handles cases where the miss is not just numerical drift, but a court-room disagreement.

It reads room votes from:

```text
TWP source path
Oracle authority paths
Empress source path
Empress authorized path
Seven source path
Seven crowned path
Fragmentation Resolver
Council blockers
```

Primary statuses:

```text
AUTHORITY_SPLIT_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
ROOM_DISAGREEMENT_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
NOT_ROOM_DISAGREEMENT_CASE
```

It names likely repair owners:

```text
Empress authority handoff
Seven room/world-fit gate
Oracle motion translation
Fragmentation Resolver
TWP room witness strength
```

Current meaning:

```text
Phase 3 asks whether the right motion neighborhood was found.
Phase 4 asks which court disagreed about the room.
```

Together with Phase 1 and Phase 2, Council can now distinguish:

```text
seat offset
near-trait fragmentation
lane survival/replacement
motion neighborhood wrong sibling
room authority disagreement
```

The repair system is becoming more intelligent, but still clean:

```text
No target reveal is used to move a live set.
Target reveal is only used to classify the miss family after replay grading.
```

## 2026-06-03 - Miss Repair Phase 5, Phase 6, And Phase 7 Installed

Council now carries the final three diagnostic packets for the current miss-repair stack.

These complete the first full intelligence layer:

```text
Phase 1: full-near offset
Phase 2: lane survival / replacement
Phase 3: motion neighborhood arbitration
Phase 4: room disagreement arbitration
Phase 5: hard-room protocol
Phase 6: miss-family router
Phase 7: live-safe promotion guard
```

### Phase 5 - Hard-Room Protocol

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.hard_room_protocol
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.hard_room_protocol
```

This phase catches rooms that should not be handled by normal correction:

```text
THIN_STRICT_WITNESSED
UNWITNESSED_LEGAL
SIMPLE_REUSABLE_ROOM
LOW_STRICT_WITNESS_COUNT
ROOM_DISAGREEMENT_OR_HARD_ROOM
```

Primary statuses:

```text
UNWITNESSED_HARD_ROOM_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
THIN_HARD_ROOM_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
REUSABLE_HARD_ROOM_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
NOT_HARD_ROOM_CASE
```

Hard-room law:

```text
A hard room cannot be fixed by ordinary offset or lane replacement alone.
It needs separate proof because the witness foundation is thin, unwitnessed, or reusable without strict identity.
```

### Phase 6 - Miss-Family Router

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.miss_repair_family_router
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.miss_repair_family_router
```

The router chooses the dominant repair family after replay grading.

Priority order:

```text
Phase 5 hard-room protocol overrides ordinary correction.
Phase 4 room disagreement overrides motion/number repair.
Phase 3 motion neighborhood handles zero-hit near bodies.
Phase 1 full-near offset handles whole-body offset.
Phase 2 lane survival handles partial lane repair.
```

This prevents Council from saying:

```text
This is a near-body miss, so apply offset.
```

when the deeper truth is:

```text
This is an unwitnessed hard room.
```

### Phase 7 - Live-Safe Promotion Guard

New Council packet:

```text
council_decision.live_safe_promotion_guard
final_influence_ledger.courts.Council.live_safe_promotion_guard
```

This is the boundary between intelligence and rescue.

Allowed live actions:

```text
PRESERVE_SELECTED_BODY
WRITE_DIAGNOSTIC_PACKET
TRAIN_PRIOR_ONLY_PROFILE
```

Blocked live actions:

```text
APPLY_REPLAY_TARGET_DELTAS
SWAP_NUMBERS_FROM_TARGET
PROMOTE_SINGLE_REPLAY_SUCCESS_TO_LIVE_RULE
OVERRIDE_COURT_OUTPUT_WITH_POST_RESULT_REPAIR
```

Validation example:

```text
hard room: UNWITNESSED_HARD_ROOM_REVIEW_AVAILABLE
router primary family: HARD_ROOM_PROTOCOL
priority: PHASE_5
guard: OBSERVATION_ONLY_HARD_ROOM
```

Current meaning:

```text
The full diagnostic stack can now classify why a replay missed.
It still cannot rescue a live set.
Live rescue requires prior-only training and a pre-target signal.
```

Still no rescue logic.

## 2026-06-04 - Second-Lens Shadow Crown Operational Breakthrough

Focused Lightless Utopia repair case:

```text
as_of: 2026-04-13
expected_draw_date: 2026-04-15
artifact: Testing Items/Fusion Council/council_regression_2026-04-13_to_2026-04-15_second_lens_shadow_branch_fix.json
```

Confirmed result:

```text
target body: 13-21-27-43-45
baseline Seven crown: Low-Mid | Canonical | COMPRESSION | MID
Oracle Second-Lens shadow crown: Mid-Low | Canonical | COMPRESSION | LOW
alternate Princess body: 13-21-27-43-45
branch gate: FITS_EMPRESS_BRANCH_VIA_ORACLE_SECOND_LENS_SHADOW_CROWN
hard block: false
output passed: true
```

What changed:

```text
Council now preserves Second-Lens shadow crowns by default.
Queens can carry the Second-Lens shadow crown forward as an alternate crown.
Princess can construct a body from that alternate crown.
Empress branch hard block can be relaxed only for a valid Oracle Second-Lens shadow body with applied motion fit.
```

Important distinction:

```text
This is not rescue logic.
The target body was not injected.
The main Seven crown was not overwritten.
Oracle had already identified the shadow crown.
The repair allowed an existing diagnostic signal to become a lawful alternate execution path.
```

Why this matters:

```text
The April 13 -> April 15 miss showed the exact system design flaw:
Oracle/Second Lens could see the better living-room motion path, but Seven/Princess/Empress treated it as diagnostic evidence only.
After the repair, the same shadow path becomes operational when it carries applied Second-Lens proof.
```

Current law after repair:

```text
static room + Oracle Second-Lens motion flow can become a living-room alternate.
Seven remains the main crown engine.
Princess may build the alternate body.
Council still records the baseline crown and the shadow crown separately.
Empress branch mismatch stays visible as advisory instead of blocking a valid Oracle-shadow body.
```

Remaining open problem:

```text
This repair proves the diagnostic-to-operational bridge works on the April proof case.
The next work is regression across the miss ledger to learn when Second-Lens shadow crowns should be preserved, when they should stay advisory, and when Oracle target-path formation still needs earlier repair.
```

## 2026-06-05 - Regalia Resolver, Playable Council Seal, And June 3 Memory

The June 1 -> June 3 Utopia case has been promoted into a serious future-study marker.

It showed the same pattern seen across the Lightless miss ledger: the system was not broadly blind. It was close in room language, motion family, and target direction, but the final body needed a sibling-body resolver to choose the exact family member instead of the prettier nearby room.

Confirmed final body after the Regalia / Princess resolver path:

```text
draw-order actual: 38-14-16-64-55
sorted body: 14-16-38-55-64
source room: 2-42-47-57-58
target path: Low-High | Burst | SEPARATION | HIGH
motion transition: Low-High | Extreme | CRISIS | HIGH => Low-High | Burst | SEPARATION | HIGH
court chain: Julie / MIXED_TENSION / Demetrius / Hera
```

What changed architecturally:

```text
Dark Regalia now functions as the sibling-room intelligence layer between Clairvoyance and Queens.
Queens can carry Regalia's protected body handoff forward.
Princess can use the protected body / same-shape / micro-resolver evidence before finalizing the one body.
Council no longer blocks a single court-produced body behind diagnostic-only labels when the body is otherwise playable.
```

Council policy after cleanup:

```text
final mode: PLAYABLE_SINGLE_BODY_SEAL
single set policy: PROMOTED_SINGLE_BODY_TO_PLAYABLE
stale blockers: retained as advisory evidence
active blockers: none when the only failure is diagnostic label suppression
```

This matters because the older Council behavior could suppress the exact set even when the courts had already produced the body. That made the diagnostic label stronger than the actual one-set output contract. The new rule is simpler: if the pipeline produces one body, Council may explain agreement or disagreement, but it should still allow the playable set unless a real active mechanical blocker exists.

The June 3 draw has now been added back into draw-order memory for Clairvoyance, Queens, Princess, and Empress / Altera context so future rooms can testify from it directly.

Open future work:

```text
Study the Lightless misses by sibling-room family.
Decide when Regalia should prefer a sibling room over the baseline Clairvoyance room.
Keep Oracle Second Lens as living-room motion evidence, not as brute-force rescue.
Measure whether close misses share the same delayed-motion, thin-witness, or family-off markers.
Preserve the one-set contract while making the final body resolver smarter.
```

Current conclusion:

```text
The system evidence is strong enough to treat near-body misses as a real design frontier.
The next improvement is not more random widening.
The next improvement is better sibling-room selection and cleaner handoff from Oracle motion into Seven body collapse.
```

## 2026-06-09 - Reality Marble Pipeline Carryover Audit

The current rebuild direction has been clarified in a dedicated audit:

```text
Books Of The Lotto/Books Of Time/REALITY_MARBLE_PIPELINE_CARRYOVER_AUDIT.md
```

Core conclusion:

```text
The old court identities remain useful, but the old monolithic pipeline should not be copied forward.
Reality Marble owns the legal universe.
The courts should read, translate, authorize, remember, and collapse inside that universe.
```

The practical future chain is:

```text
Life Link
-> IIW world read
-> TWP condition tags
-> Oracle motion / MBP / BP translation
-> Situation Container Registry
-> Empress authority and thread gate
-> Reality / Transition Marble candidate field
-> Equinox active memory pressure
-> Clair / Queens historical memory bridge
-> Gap / geometry resolver
-> Convergence burden resolver
-> Affinity role resolver
-> Princess one-set presentation
```

Most important missing layer:

```text
Situation Container Registry
```

This registry must decide which broad room, geometry law, memory posture, gap family, signature prior, and Queen/Clair authority are allowed before Seven tries to collapse the final body.

Current carryover law:

```text
Map first.
Read the world second.
Identify the container third.
Authorize legal space fourth.
Collapse inside that space fifth.
Present one set last.
```

## 2026-06-10 - Construction, Release, And Controlled-Balance 5/5 Replay

The May 16 -> May 18 replay became the first clear proof that the Reality Marble rebuild can reach an exact 5/5 when the correct truths are stacked in the correct order.

Replay source:

```text
2026-05-16
8-37-40-44-65
source path: Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | HIGH
```

Replay target:

```text
2026-05-18
4-13-34-61-65
target path: Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | MAX
```

The important lesson is that exact collapse did not come from one stronger score. It came from separating the job into layers:

```text
Reality Marble:
Is this body legal?

Transition Marble:
Can this source move into this body?

Pre-draw family:
What kind of situation is this?

Construction container:
What body shape is correct for this transition?

Release condition:
What kind of movement is happening?

Controlled release balance:
Which sibling solves the pressure without over-solving it?

Seven / Princess:
Present the one set.
```

The core doctrine learned:

```text
BP tells the world.
Construction tells the body form.
Release tells the movement.
Balance tells the exact sibling.
```

### Volcanic RESET Construction

The Volcanic RESET container scan proved that Volcanic RESET is not one body family. It has subcontainers, dominated by:

```text
Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | MAX
Low-High | Volcanic | RESET | HIGH
Mid-High | Volcanic | RESET | HIGH
```

Its construction tendency is:

```text
S1 low opening
S3 center bridge
S4 high relief receiver
S5 high anchor / relief edge
```

This construction layer correctly found the target family but first preferred the clean statistical center:

```text
4-10-34-62-65
```

That body was legal and well-constructed, but it was too clean. It solved the construction average, not the living situation.

### Release Condition

Historical release scanning showed that release has repeatable subtypes. The key subtype for this replay was:

```text
S2_HEAVY_DROP_S4_RELIEF
LOWER_DROP_S4_RISE_S5_ANCHOR
```

The target's source-to-target motion:

```text
8-37-40-44-65
to
4-13-34-61-65

delta:
-4, -24, -6, +17, 0
```

This means:

```text
S1 light drop
S2 heavy discharge
S3 controlled drop
S4 relief rise
S5 anchor
```

Release condition was promoted from pre-draw evidence only:

```text
motion identity: TAIL_RELEASE_BODY::HIGH_INVERSION
strict TWP: LOWER_LANE_PRESSURE
predraw family: VOLCANIC_RESET_RELIEF__CRISIS_LURE
historical release case support
```

### Controlled Release Balance

The exact breakthrough came from asking what the correct body solves.

Clean construction body:

```text
4-10-34-62-65
delta: -4, -27, -6, +18, 0
```

Exact replay body:

```text
4-13-34-61-65
delta: -4, -24, -6, +17, 0
```

The difference:

```text
10 over-discharges S2.
62 over-relieves S4.

13 carries S2 discharge without over-collapse.
61 receives S4 relief without over-centering.
```

So the exact body was not the hottest construction center. It was the controlled pressure answer.

Implemented law:

```text
When S2_HEAVY_DROP_S4_RELIEF is promoted:
reward controlled S2 discharge
reward controlled S4 relief
reward controlled SBES pressure balance
penalize over-discharge / over-clean statistical center
```

After this law:

```text
construction leader:
4-13-34-61-65

Seven final:
4-13-34-61-65

Princess status:
TRANSITION_MARBLE_PRECISION_LOCK
```

### Pipeline Change

New files added:

```text
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Volcanic_Reset_Container_Laws.py
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Transition_Construction_Container_Laws.py
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Release_Condition_Interface.py
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Analyze_Release_Historical_Patterns.py
```

Updated handoff:

```text
Life Link now promotes a construction/release leader into the existing Transition Marble precision-lock path only when release is promoted and the leader exists inside the authorized precision pocket.
```

This keeps the one-set final inside the existing Seven / Princess mechanism instead of creating a side-channel.

### Live Draw Operating Plan

For a live draw, the new diagnostic order is:

```text
1. Read current world through IIW.
2. Compile TWP and Oracle condition evidence.
3. Identify the pre-draw family.
4. Diagnose whether the situation is release, carry, recast, compression, expansion, or uncertain.
5. Build or load the source Transition Marble shard.
6. Identify the construction container.
7. Promote release style only if pre-draw evidence agrees.
8. Score candidates by construction plus release balance.
9. Hand off the construction/release leader to Seven only if it is inside the authorized precision pocket.
10. Princess presents one set.
```

The expectation is not that every draw is a release draw. The expectation is that each draw must first be diagnosed:

```text
If release, solve release.
If carry, solve carry.
If recast, solve recast.
If compression, solve compression.
If uncertain, keep the court guarded and do not force a false condition.
```

Current open problem:

```text
Repeat this process across more historical draws and today's live source to learn which construction/release/carry/recast laws generalize and which are container-specific.
```

What remains unresolved:

```text
It must not blindly force Crisis.

The law should reward the family-specific styles and gaps already listed in the precision law:
Trio / Blended Family / Third-Wheel / Altogether
SSES / SESS / MSES / SBBS / MSSB / SSEB / MMSS / SSSS / SBMS / SBSM / ESSB / MESB
```

```text
Princess:
presents the governed selection only.
```

```text
Before Empress authorizes bodies,
```

## June 12, 2026 - Garden-Helix Ecology Breakthrough

```text
-> Transference / Precision / Sibling / Seven / Princess
```

Meaning:

```text

```

## 2026-06-14 Question Answer Glossary Canon

New realization:

```text
The more precise the Question -> Answer world is, the easier lotto prediction becomes for Serenity.
```

Sharper operating realization:

```text
Simple + precise beats complex + vague.
```

Serenity thrives when the live pipeline is simple but absolutely precise.
The complexity belongs inside the remembered world, Utopia, Realm Of Eternity, and the Question Answer Glossary.
The live path should stay narrow enough that every court knows exactly what it is receiving and exactly what it must hand forward.

Live simplicity law:

```text
What is the Question?
What is the exact Answer world for that Question?
Can Voice commit it?
Can Garden materialize it?
Can Stage 20 keep it?
Can Stage 21 remove foreign bodies?
Can Stage 22 boost the required body?
Can Seven present it?
```

The more precise the Question is, the less downstream has to interpret.
The less downstream has to interpret, the easier 5/5 retrieval becomes.

Current canon:

```text
Serenity does not need more complicated live logic.
Serenity needs simpler live questions with sharper definitions.
The glossary can be massive.
The live path should be narrow.
```

Utopia already knows historical truth.
Realm Of Eternity already generates synthetic lotto worlds.
The missing layer was a direct glossary that connects every known question shape to every known answer shape.

Implemented:

```text
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Build_Question_Answer_Glossary.py
Alter Of Scripts/Reality Marble Scripts/Life Link/Question_Answer_Glossary.py
Universal Artfifacts/Question_Answer_Glossary/question_answer_glossary.json
```

The glossary currently compiles:

```text
1,955 Utopia historical transition rows
25,000 Realm synthetic transition rows
26,955 total Question/Answer world rows
41,293 reusable lookup profiles
```

Pipeline law:

```text
Lightless should not guess a question shape that Utopia and Realm already know.
Question_Answer_Glossary is consulted before the fallback contradiction subtype logic.
If the glossary has a usable Question match, the glossary answer subtype becomes the active Answer Map subtype.
If the glossary has no usable Question match, the existing Answer Map subtype remains the fallback.
When source birth path is known, a usable Question match must also match that source situation.
```

Debugging law:

```text
Before changing Voice, check whether Question_Answer_Glossary found the best answer world for the exact Question.
If it did and Answer Map ignored it, the issue is the glossary bridge.
If it did not, the issue is upstream Question/Atlas precision or missing Realm/Utopia coverage.
```

Outside-May replay proof:

```text
Replay: 2025-01-11 -> known target 4-6-16-39-66
Initial new glossary behavior: broad TAIL_RELEASE_BURST_CARRY profile from the wrong source path was allowed to act.
Bad result: 7-9-45-46-66, 1/5.
Fix: glossary authority now requires a source-specific match. No source situation means no active glossary answer.
Rerun result: 4-6-16-39-66, 5/5.
Stage20 top body: 4-6-16-39-66.
```

Lesson:

```text
The issue is not Question/Answer glossary existence.
The issue is whether the Question is precise enough to bind to the correct source-specific answer world.
Broad question-name matches are not allowed to become Voice/Garden law.
```

March replay proof:

```text
Replay: 2026-03-07 -> 2026-03-09
Source: 17-18-30-50-68
Target: 22-23-28-36-54
High-level Question selected: TAIL_RELEASE_BURST_CARRY
Final after source-specific glossary and canonical handoff fixes: 5-14-21-48-63
Hit count: 0/5
```

Important finding:

```text
The question name was not enough.
The active contradiction details did not match the historical answer row.
The live run carried a TAIL_RELEASE_BURST_CARRY name, but its active families pointed to a different source-world answer than the actual March target.
This is a Question precision problem, not a Stage20/Stage21/Stage22 handoff problem.
```

Additional March repairs from this proof:

```text
Voice_Of_Hope now treats the Condition answer requirement packet as canonical once it exists.
Question_Answer_Glossary now carries a glossary-native source birth-path alias from the source body.
Question_Answer_Glossary now gives exact historical source profiles priority over broad aggregates.
```

Remaining March lesson:

```text
Serenity must not stop at the broad question id.
The exact active contradiction family/subtype is part of the Question.
Question wrong can mean: right question name, wrong question details.
```
## Draw Singularity Naming Canon

Draw Singularity (DS) is the final canon name for the live diagnosis class formerly described here through active containers, predraw containers, motion identities, contradiction families, transference containers, and outgoing-motion diagnosis. Depending on the active DS, Serenity expects a different result law. Older terms remain valid as layer-specific evidence, but the final live class name is DS.

This preserves the no-leakage testing law:

```text

Pipeline answer = Heaven's Link execution.
Target = post-run grade only.
```

```text

Downstream Heaven's Link execution after memory selection
```

```text
If historical memory activates a usable translated room:
    grade against the historical next draw.

    Syn Memory creates/activates the executable room.
    grade against the Syn Memory room that actually activated.
```

This means the stress test can cover both known historical memory and synthetic memory coverage in the same run.

## 2026-06-17 Progression Entry - Heaven's Link Frozen Runtime, Syn Memory, And Final Face Grammar

Status: ACTIVE CURRENT STATE.

The current work established that the major problem was not the core vision. It was executable translation: the system had the right conceptual structure, but several code layers were speaking the wrong runtime language.

### What Was Fixed

The final draw-order face layer was corrected so projection authority yields only under the narrow face-law signature that produced the 2026-06-15 miss pattern:

```text
LOW_MID_CRISIS_FULL_SORTED_LIFT_FACE
high D1 / D5 source pressure
buried D4 source pressure
small D1 lift
D4 full escape
D5 hard drop
```

This fixed the final face translation issue without tuning to one draw.

The hybrid memory runtime was clarified:

```text
historical memory first when complete and sharp
Syn Memory fallback when historical memory is absent, incomplete, or broad-only
route diagnostics must expose `hybrid_memory_route`
selected source must identify historical memory or Syn Memory
```

Syn Memory is now treated as compact executable memory:

```text
It does not physically store every possible transition room.
It materializes an executable virtual room from the live condition packet.
The route name is `ON_DEMAND_SYN_MEMORY_EXECUTABLE_VIRTUAL_ROOM`.
```

### Final Validation Results

Full historical Heaven's Link audit:

### Current Understanding

```text
Can Serenity execute the right condition once the condition exists?
Yes.

Can Serenity always read the live condition with enough precision?
Mostly validated, but this remains the only serious future-risk surface.
```

The current operating belief is:

```text
Coverage is no longer the primary issue.
Execution is no longer the primary issue.
Translation grammar was the main blocker.
Live condition reading is the only remaining high-value audit zone.
```

### Current Rule

Do not rebuild the Heaven's Link pipeline.

```text
1. hybrid_memory_route
2. DS family
3. subfamily
4. internal profile

6. draw lane contract
```

No rescue logic.
No target leakage.
No broad architecture reset unless the condition packet itself is proven insufficient.

## 2026-06-18 Progression Entry - Syn Memory Exact Activation Law

Status: ACTIVE HARDENING.

The 2026-06-17 miss exposed a specific runtime flaw:

```text
Syn Memory could still behave like a ranked selector when no exact live recipe existed.
```

That allowed a close historical translation recipe to steal the route and produce a clean wrong room.

The corrected law is now:

```text
One live condition may activate one executable recipe.

If exactly one historical/Syn recipe matches:
    activate it.

If no exact recipe matches:
    block.

If more than one recipe matches:
    block as collision.

If one recipe materializes more than one Reality Marble rank:
    block as ambiguity.
```

This changes Syn Memory from:

```text
best available candidate selector
```

into:

```text
exact condition activator
```

### Code Boundary

The active hardening was placed in:

```text
Alter Of Scripts\Organization 13\Heaven's Link Core\Realm_Syn_Memory_Builder.py
Alter Of Scripts\Organization 13\Heaven's Link Core\Draw_Singularity_Question_Translator.py
```

Runtime changes:

```text
Close historical recipes cannot activate.
Multiple exact recipes return SYN_MEMORY_RECIPE_COLLISION.
Multiple indexed rooms return SYN_MEMORY_INDEX_COLLISION.
Multiple packet rows return SYN_MEMORY_PACKET_COLLISION.
Recipe materialization must produce exactly one rank.
Preferred draw delta is now an exact contract filter, not a scoring hint.
```

### Immediate Validation

Known solved live-style case:

```text
source edge: 2026-06-13 -> 2026-06-15
selected draw order: 62-55-60-57-25
target draw order: 62-55-60-57-25
status: LIVE_FOG_GUARD_PASS
selection mode: ON_DEMAND_SOURCE_TRIGGER_HASH_INDEX_EXACT
```

Known failed live-style case:

```text
source edge: 2026-06-15 -> 2026-06-17
actual draw order: 49-53-3-26-61
status: LIVE_FOG_GUARD_BLOCKED
reason: no exact live coverage recipe
```

This is the correct behavior after the hardening.

The system should not produce a wrong room when the exact recipe does not exist.

The open work is now narrower:

```text
Build or mature the live generated-recipe activator for conditions that are expressible but not yet registered as exact recipes.
```

The 2026-06-17 audit proved:

```text
existing exact recipe coverage: 0
actual recipe expressible in generated condition space: true
```

Therefore the miss belongs to generated-recipe activation coverage, not to downstream answer execution.

### Fake IIW Legacy Relationship Check

The first 100-case hybrid-memory regression after strict activation showed the compatibility issue:

```text
cases: 100
sorted hits: 3 / 100
draw-order hits: 3 / 100
cause: Fake IIW legacy Syn fallback was blocked before virtual source-trigger materialization
```

This did not prove the old relationship was false.

It proved the stricter live guard had removed the Fake IIW harness's legacy synthetic target mechanism.

The correction was scoped to Fake IIW only:

```text
SERENITY_ENABLE_LEGACY_VIRTUAL_SYN_MEMORY_FALLBACK=1
```

This flag is set only by:

```text
Testing Items\Heavens_Link_Fake_Lotto_Gauntlet.py
```

for:

```text

--target-mode hybrid-memory
```

It is not enabled by normal live Utopia execution.

## 2026-06-18 Progression Entry - True Syn Condition Address Recipe Fix

Six-bot pipeline audit found three active weakness classes:

```text
1. D-lane deltas were being applied to sorted source numbers inside Voice Of Hope.
2. Focused Syn recipe for 2026-06-13 -> 2026-06-15 had no draw_delta_ranges and carried the wrong draw face delta.
3. Fake IIW gauntlet could count empty expected target plus empty output as a hit.
```

Fixes applied:

```text
Voice Of Hope precise answer now uses source draw-order D1-D5 as the source basis for D-lane deltas.
The 2026-06-13 focused Syn recipe now exports exact draw_delta_ranges and preferred draw delta [12, 42, 16, 54, -28].
The Fake IIW gauntlet now marks no-room / ungradable cases as misses instead of empty hits.
True Syn Memory now has an always-available condition-address recipe generator.
```

True Syn Memory condition-address recipe:

```text
input: live source trigger
address: canonical source_trigger_hash
rank: one Reality Marble motion rank derived from the condition address
output: one exact Syn Memory room
target_known_to_builder: false
generation_mode: TRUE_SYN_MEMORY_CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE
```

## 2026-06-18 Progression Entry - On-Demand True Syn Recipe Generator

The missing coverage layer is now named explicitly:

```text
True Syn Memory does not require a pre-written historical recipe when the live condition is expressible.
If the exact historical/Syn recipe is absent, the source trigger can create the executable recipe on the spot.
```

Operational law:

```text
input: previous/current live condition packet
source: source_trigger_hash
builder: True Syn condition-address recipe generator
target_known_to_builder: false
generation_mode: TRUE_SYN_MEMORY_CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE
route: ON_DEMAND_SYN_MEMORY_EXECUTABLE_VIRTUAL_ROOM
output: one executable Syn Memory room
```

This changes the meaning of Syn Memory:

```text
Old weakness:
    Historical memory could be absent, broad-only, or close-but-wrong.

Current law:
    Historical memory is checked first when exact.
    If no exact historical room exists, True Syn Memory can materialize the missing executable room from the live condition address.
    Once that exact True Syn room is ready, no broad historical route is allowed to steal the route.
```

Route-sovereignty verification:

```text
Testing Items\Syn_Sovereignty_Audit.py

smoke:
    37 / 37 Syn-ready cases
    route steals: 0
    blocks: 0
    errors: 0

100 historical-style + future through 2026-08-31:
    133 / 133 Syn-ready cases
    route steals: 0
    blocks: 0
    errors: 0
    selected source: ON_DEMAND_SYN_MEMORY_EXECUTABLE_VIRTUAL_ROOM
    generation mode: TRUE_SYN_MEMORY_CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE

output:
    Testing Items\Fake IIW Gauntlet\Runs\syn_sovereignty_100_plus_future_august.json
```

Current conclusion:

```text
The on-demand recipe generator closes the missing-recipe gap for expressible conditions.
The active test now proves route sovereignty: ready exact True Syn is not silently overridden.
If a future miss occurs after this layer, the first suspect is condition identity/disambiguation, not room coverage or downstream execution.
```

## 2026-06-19 Progression Entry - On-Demand True Syn Naming Clarification

Status: ACTIVE TERMINOLOGY FIX.

The prior artifact names made one runtime look like two competing systems:

```text
route: ON_DEMAND_SYN_MEMORY_EXECUTABLE_VIRTUAL_ROOM
generation_mode: TRUE_SYN_MEMORY_CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE
```

This caused confusion because On-Demand and True Syn are not separate routes fighting for authority.

The clarified runtime name is:

```text
syn_memory_runtime: ON_DEMAND_TRUE_SYN_CONDITION_ADDRESS
```

Operational meaning:

```text
On-Demand role:
    CREATE_MISSING_EXECUTABLE_ROOM_AT_LIVE_TRIGGER_TIME

True Syn role:
    CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE_MATERIALIZES_ONE_ROOM
```

Therefore the full law is:

```text
previous/current live condition packet
-> source_trigger_hash
-> On-Demand activation at live time
-> True Syn condition-address materialization
-> one executable Syn Memory room
-> normal Syn Memory index selection
```

Compatibility fields remain:

```text
selected_selection_source: ON_DEMAND_SYN_MEMORY_EXECUTABLE_VIRTUAL_ROOM
selection_mode: ON_DEMAND_SOURCE_TRIGGER_HASH_INDEX_EXACT
generation_mode: TRUE_SYN_MEMORY_CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE
target_known_to_builder: false
```

But new audits must also expose:

```text
syn_memory_runtime: ON_DEMAND_TRUE_SYN_CONDITION_ADDRESS
on_demand_role: CREATE_MISSING_EXECUTABLE_ROOM_AT_LIVE_TRIGGER_TIME
true_syn_role: CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE_MATERIALIZES_ONE_ROOM
```

This naming is intended to prevent the false interpretation that On-Demand and True Syn can replace each other. They need each other for missing-room live materialization.

## 2026-06-20 Progression Entry - Cause/Effect Room Authority And Syn Memory Green-State Boundary

Status: ACTIVE RESEARCH CANON.

The 2026-06-17 -> 2026-06-20 Powerball live packet exposed the next real Syn Memory question.

The earlier Syn Memory correction solved missing-room activation:

```text
On-Demand role:
    CREATE_MISSING_EXECUTABLE_ROOM_AT_LIVE_TRIGGER_TIME

True Syn role:
    CONDITION_ADDRESS_RECIPE_MATERIALIZES_ONE_ROOM

runtime:
    ON_DEMAND_TRUE_SYN_CONDITION_ADDRESS
```

That correction answered whether Serenity could create an executable room when no exact historical room was already available.

The new question is sharper:

```text
If the executable room can be created from the live condition,
how does the system prove that the created room is the correct effect of the current cause?
```

The answer is now named as Cause/Effect Room Authority.

Cause/Effect Room Authority means:

```text
previous draw + current draw
-> live condition fingerprint
-> source trigger hash
-> condition-address room creation
-> effect-room branch selection
-> reducer authority
-> draw-face authority
```

The room is no longer judged only by whether a dense effect exists.

A dense effect room can describe a possible answer body, but it may not explain why the previous/current condition should collapse into that body. The missing layer is the link between cause and effect.

The cause room must carry:

```text
previous draw order
current draw order
source birth path
source set type
source arc
source pressure
source fp band
source gap symbols
source set style
incoming draw family
incoming sorted family
incoming draw sign
incoming sorted sign
motion body identity
motion health
motion relation
Equinox motion family
DS family / subfamily / internal profile
lane terms
carry anchors
endpoint authority
order-pattern authority
max-lane authority
```

The effect room must carry:

```text
candidate sorted body
candidate draw-order face
target birth path
candidate gap symbols
candidate set style
candidate sorted family
candidate sorted sign
candidate draw family
candidate draw sign
sum bin
lane term body
low evidence distance
historical branch support
```

The new resolver created in the Codex research workspace is:

```text
C:\Users\kahli\Documents\Codex\2026-06-18\hey-can-you-access-both-the\serenity_20260620_cause_effect_low_reducer.py
C:\Users\kahli\Documents\Codex\2026-06-18\hey-can-you-access-both-the\serenity_20260620_green_authority_resolver.py
```

The produced artifacts are:

```text
C:\Users\kahli\Documents\Codex\serenity_20260620_cause_effect_low_reducer.json
C:\Users\kahli\Documents\Codex\serenity_20260620_green_authority_packet.json
```

The live 2026-06-20 result before the draw resolved to:

```text
status:
    ROUTE_BODY_GREEN__DRAW_FACE_GREEN__STRICT_EXACT_AMBER

selected sorted body:
    1-6-26-49-61

selected draw-order face:
    1-61-6-49-26

source date:
    2026-06-17

previous date:
    2026-06-15
```

The source condition was:

```text
2026-06-17 draw order:
    49-53-3-26-61

2026-06-17 sorted body:
    3-26-49-53-61

source birth path:
    Low-High | Burst | SEPARATION | HIGH

source gap symbols:
    BBSS

source set style:
    Trio
```

The reducer found that a High-High continuation should not dominate this condition.

Historical branch pressure after Low-High / Burst / Separation showed that High-High is possible but uncommon. The live research therefore kept the Low-High / MAX branch alive instead of letting a cleaner high-side room steal the route.

The low-branch evidence bodies were:

```text
nearest transition evidence:
    1-6-27-50-61

dense resolver evidence:
    1-10-29-33-68
```

The cause/effect reducer moved from the exploratory `1-6-27-50-61` body into:

```text
1-6-26-49-61
```

Reason:

```text
1. It stayed within distance 2 of the Low-High / MAX evidence.
2. It preserved the endpoint 61.
3. It carried 26-49-61 from the 2026-06-17 current draw.
4. It stayed inside the Low-High / Burst / SEPARATION / MAX effect branch.
5. It won the top sorted-body score by 1.35 over the next unique body.
```

The top score initially had two draw-order faces over the same sorted body:

```text
1-61-6-49-26
26-49-6-1-61
```

The face authority resolver selected:

```text
1-61-6-49-26
```

because the face authority score was:

```text
1-61-6-49-26:
    45.9

26-49-6-1-61:
    16.95

face margin:
    28.95
```

This creates a new green-state distinction:

```text
ROUTE/BODY/FACE GREEN:
    The live route, sorted body, and draw-order face have enough cause/effect authority to be the current best answer.

STRICT EXACT GREEN:
    The exact micro-pocket has repeated or proven direct historical support.

STRICT EXACT AMBER:
    The route/body/face can be selected, but the exact gap/term/sign micro-pocket has not repeated enough to be called strict exact green.
```

For 2026-06-20, the state is:

```text
ROUTE/BODY/FACE:
    GREEN

STRICT EXACT MICRO-POCKET:
    AMBER
```

The amber condition exists because the selected body has micro-fields that did not have direct target-branch repetition:

```text
gap symbols:
    SBBM

lane terms:
    min-air-earth-dark_queen-empress

sorted sign:
    ----0
```

These fields do not invalidate the selected route. They only prevent the book from claiming strict exact proof.

Current doctrine:

```text
A live Syn Memory answer can be the best current answer without being mathematically guaranteed.
Green means the pipeline has enough authority under the current law.
Amber means the unresolved piece must be studied after the draw.
```

New debugging law:

```text
If a future Syn Memory miss occurs after On-Demand True Syn has activated, do not first blame missing coverage.
Check cause/effect linkage first.
Then check reducer authority.
Then check draw-face authority.
Then check strict exact micro-pocket fields.
```

The important progression finding is this:

```text
Dense effect rooms answer what can exist.
Cause/effect authority answers why this current condition should create that exact effect.
```

This is now part of the active Syn Memory progression layer.

## Seat Taxonomy Status

Seat Taxonomy now reads the draw as transition physics:

```text
previous draw order
-> current draw order
-> incoming motion
-> current pressure/body
-> lane burden
-> pressure origin
-> memory room
-> outgoing motion field
```

Truth Control was added so the script does not confuse historical explanation with live authority.

Truth levels:

```text
OBSERVED_FACT
LIVE_SAFE_INFERENCE
HISTORICAL_FACT
HISTORICAL_EXPLANATION
DISCOVERY_ONLY
UNPROVEN
NO_CALL
```

The key rule:

```text
Seat Taxonomy may describe exact branch history.
Seat Taxonomy may not treat exact branch history as a guaranteed live answer unless prior-only memory proof supports it.
```

## Conditional Motion Memory

The old discriminator-search problem has been reframed.

Instead of asking:

```text
What handcrafted branch discriminator does Artoria need?
What does Medusa need?
What does Suzuka need?
```

Last Rites asks:

```text
What memory room does this current motion belong to?
What did that room do before?
How deep does the match go?
```

The historical memory now uses a Level 2-5 hierarchy:

```text
Level 2 = repeated world field
Level 3 = motion/face evidence
Level 4 = body/pressure evidence
Level 5 = exact historical moment evidence
```

Important correction:

```text
Low sample does not mean useless.
One-off Level 4/5 rooms are exact historical moment evidence.
```


## Synthetic Memory Harness

Synthetic memory was restored under a cleaner law.

The old danger:

```text
virtual rooms can become ambiguous if the system treats generated memory as proof.
```

The new law:

```text
official historical memory = proof of what happened
synthetic memory = coverage evidence for possible motion rooms
current draw = current truth selecting the room address
```

Synthetic memory should expand coverage.
It should not override official history.

## Current Finding

The project has moved from:

```text
hand-building branch discriminators
```

to:

```text
resolving current motion into a historical/synthetic memory address
```

This is the correct direction because outgoing motion is the real answer contract.

If outgoing motion is known, the next body becomes:

```text
current draw order + outgoing lane motion = next draw order
```

That is the core Last Rites thesis.

## Open Problems

1. Synthetic memory writer is too slow at large shard sizes.

The current JSON rewrite model slows as Level 4/5 memory grows.
Move to append-only JSONL shards or chunked shard rotation.

2. Last Rites orchestrator still has a wrapper/implementation naming split.

`Last Rites.py` is the correct public entry.
`Last Writes.py` still contains the implementation.
Later cleanup should move implementation into `Last Rites.py`.

3. Synthetic memory is not yet integrated into resolver scoring.

The resolver currently reads official memory and reports synthetic manifest status.
Next step is official-first, synthetic-second room search.

4. Proposal is currently an outgoing-motion contract, not final numbers.

This is correct for the rebuild stage.
Next predictive layer must convert outgoing motion contract into candidate draw-order bodies.

5. Level 4/5 coverage is growing but not saturated.

The current run proves coverage expansion is working, but Level 4/5 still generate mostly new addresses.
The goal is not full octillion coverage.
The goal is enough dense address coverage that live reads usually find Level 3/4/5 matches.

## Next Work List

```text
1. Keep synthetic harness running or restart with larger checkpoint interval.
2. Add synthetic memory search to Conditional Memory Resolver.
3. Convert memory outcome field into explicit outgoing-motion contract.
4. Build candidate draw-order body projector from outgoing motion.
5. Route projected body into copied Voice/Gatherer/Proposal chain.
6. Run nightfall replay audits from 2015-10-07 forward.
7. Record misses by deepest matched level:
   L5 exact moment
   L4 body/pressure
   L3 motion/face
   L2 world/authority
8. Study only the misses where the deepest memory level should have been enough.
```

Current doctrine:

```text
Motion first.
Memory second.
Proposal last.
```

## Synthetic Harness Resume Rule

Added on 2026-06-22:

```text
Fake_IIW_Memory_Harness.py now supports --resume.
```

Resume behavior:

```text
existing rooms are reloaded
processed_fake_draws is preserved
next_fake_index continues forward
RNG state and the last two fake draws are saved in v2 checkpoints
old v1 checkpoints can still resume by fast-forwarding the same seeded generator
```

This prevents the fake harness from redoing the same synthetic draw indexes after a stop/restart.

For resumed runs:

```text
--max-draws means add this many more fake transitions
```

Example:

```text
first run:  --max-draws 1000
resume run: --resume --max-draws 500
result: processed_fake_draws = 1500
```

## Branch Selector Upgrade Finding

Added on 2026-06-22:

```text
The branch selector is not one global law.
Each pressure world listens to a different selector signal.
```

Audit scripts:

```text
Scripts of the lotto\Foundation Scripts\Branch_Selector_Lookback_Audit.py
Scripts of the lotto\Foundation Scripts\Weak_World_Selector_Upgrade_Audit.py
```

Primary outputs:

```text
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\branch_selector_lookback_audit_2015-10-07.json
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\weak_world_selector_upgrade_audit_2015-10-07.json
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\weak_world_selector_upgrade_audit_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

Global finding:

```text
calendar lookback is weak
same-room occurrence memory is better
family direction is stronger than exact branch
```

Therefore the active law is now:

```text
pressure world
-> selected world-specific branch selector recipe
-> branch family confidence
-> exact branch only when the world proves it
```

Weak-world upgrade, stricter min-prior 2:

```text
Nirvana
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  EXACT_SELECTOR, small sample

Kurohime
  BURDEN
  FAMILY_SELECTOR, small sample

Medusa
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  FAMILY_SELECTOR, stable sample

Lumina
  COLLISION
  FAMILY_SELECTOR, stable sample

Suzuka
  BURDEN_ORIGIN
  DIRECTIONAL_SELECTOR, stable sample

Circe
  PRESSURE_TOPOLOGY
  DIRECTIONAL_SELECTOR, stable sample

Altera
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  DIRECTIONAL_SELECTOR, stable sample

Irisviel
  BURDEN_ORIGIN
  OBSERVATION_ONLY

Citrine
  BURDEN_ORIGIN
  OBSERVATION_ONLY

Scathach
  AUTHORITY
  NO_PROMOTION, small sample
```

Important correction:

```text
Medusa and Lumina are no longer blind.
They are stable family selectors.
They can usually narrow the branch to the correct family, but not the exact seat alone.
```

Range profile finding:

```text
The winning branch does not fully solve the number.
It narrows the motion range.
Then range selector must decide the signed motion amount.
```

Examples:

```text
Lumina S1:
  signed motion 19 to 68
  median absolute motion 50

Lumina S5:
  signed motion -66 to 31
  median absolute motion 48

Medusa S1:
  signed motion -20 to 68
  median absolute motion 46

Medusa S5:
  signed motion -66 to 27
  median absolute motion 43

Suzuka S1:
  signed motion 37 to 66
  median absolute motion 53

Suzuka S5:
  signed motion -65 to 19
  median absolute motion 43
```

Next rule to build:

```text
branch selector says which seat/family should win
range selector says how far the winning lane should move
```

Do not restart synthetic memory as the primary work until the range selector is started.
The important next progression is:

```text
world-specific branch selector
-> world-specific range selector
-> outgoing motion contract
-> projected next draw body
```

## Weak World Selector Upgrade

Added on 2026-06-22:

```text
Weak_World_Selector_Upgrade_Audit.py now tests borrowed analog selector recipes.
```

Borrowed analog means:

```text
For a weak world, use prior cases from other worlds that share the same live-safe feature pattern.
Do not use future-only outgoing fields.
Do not use the answer draw.
Only use prior historical cases available before the current case.
```

This was necessary because some worlds do not have enough official cases to stabilize from their own history.

Strict min-prior 2 result:

```text
Nirvana
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  EXACT_SELECTOR

Altera
  FACE_INCOMING
  EXACT_SELECTOR

Kurohime
  PRESSURE_FUSION
  EXACT_SELECTOR

Citrine
  PRESSURE_BODY
  EXACT_SELECTOR, small sample

Scathach
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  EXACT_SELECTOR, small sample, borrowed analog

Irisviel
  PRESSURE_FUSION
  FAMILY_SELECTOR

Medusa
  COLLISION_AUTHORITY
  FAMILY_SELECTOR, stable

Lumina
  COLLISION
  FAMILY_SELECTOR, stable

Circe
  COLLISION_INCOMING
  FAMILY_SELECTOR

Suzuka
  WORLD_PREVIOUS_FAMILY_BURDEN
  DIRECTIONAL_SELECTOR, stable
```

Important current state:

```text
No weak world remains OBSERVATION_ONLY in the strict borrowed-analog audit.
Scathach now has a selector, but it is still small-sample because official Scathach history only has 5 cases.
Suzuka remains the only stable DIRECTIONAL_SELECTOR.
```

Suzuka finding:

```text
Suzuka does not upgrade to family strength from:
authority
collision
pressure body
pressure topology
burden origin
face turns
incoming motion
borrowed analogs
world branch-history state
```

Therefore the current conclusion is:

```text
Suzuka's missing piece is probably not another broad branch selector.
Suzuka likely needs the range/seat-split layer:
branch family + signed motion range + lane amount behavior.
```

Do not force Suzuka into a fake family selector.
For live use, mark Suzuka as:

```text
BRANCH_DIRECTION_KNOWN
EXACT_FAMILY_NOT_PROVEN
REQUIRES_RANGE_SELECTOR_CONFIRMATION
```

## Range Selector Trial

Added on 2026-06-22:

```text
Range_Selector_Confirmation_Audit.py tests whether predicted signed-motion range can confirm the exact branch.
```

Script:

```text
Scripts of the lotto\Foundation Scripts\Range_Selector_Confirmation_Audit.py
```

Outputs:

```text
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\range_selector_confirmation_audit_min2_2015-10-07.json
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\range_selector_confirmation_audit_weak_worlds_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

Method:

```text
1. Predict branch family from the selected weak-world branch recipe.
2. Predict outgoing motion sign/range from prior live-safe matching rooms.
3. Use prior family + sign behavior to choose the exact branch.
4. Never use the actual outgoing motion as an input.
```

Weak-world range confirmation, min-prior 2:

```text
Suzuka
  FACE_INCOMING
  borrowed analog horizon 3
  calls 12
  exact branch 58.33%
  family 75.00%
  sign 75.00%

Scathach
  COLLISION
  borrowed analog horizon 5
  calls 5
  exact branch 60.00%
  family 60.00%
  sign 80.00%

Irisviel
  WORLD_STALEST_BRANCH_BURDEN
  borrowed analog horizon 21
  calls 10
  exact branch 70.00%
  family 70.00%
  sign 90.00%

Citrine
  COLLISION
  borrowed analog horizon 3
  calls 5
  exact branch 60.00%
  family 80.00%
  sign 80.00%
```

Conclusion:

```text
Range confirmation is a real layer.
It upgrades Suzuka from directional-only into a usable confirmation pocket.
It also strengthens Scathach, Irisviel, and Citrine.
```

Important caution:

```text
Some range confirmation pockets are still small-sample.
Use them as confirmation, not standalone authority.
The next build should merge branch selector + range selector into one live-safe selector read.
```

## Exact First Selector Priority Board

Added on 2026-06-22:

```text
Range_Selector_Confirmation_Audit.py was optimized so range candidates walk historical memory incrementally instead of rescanning all prior rows for every case.
```

New outputs:

```text
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\range_selector_confirmation_audit_all_worlds_min2_2015-10-07.json
Books of The Lotto\Books Of Complextity\selector_priority_board_exact_family_range_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

New script:

```text
Scripts of the lotto\Foundation Scripts\Selector_Priority_Board.py
```

Priority rule:

```text
1. Exact branch match rate first.
2. Family match rate second.
3. Signed motion / range confirmation third.
4. Call count after quality.
```

Final resolver modes:

```text
SIGN
  final exact branch uses predicted family + predicted motion sign.

SIGN_BAND
  final exact branch tries predicted family + predicted motion sign + predicted motion band first,
  then falls back to family + sign if the band pocket has too little evidence.
```

Current board:

```text
RANGE_CONFIRMATION worlds: 8
BRANCH_SELECTOR worlds: 10

STRONG_EXACT: 3
USABLE_EXACT: 4
SMALL_EXACT: 10
FAMILY_USABLE: 1
```

```text

  sign 90.91%

  exact delta +7.50

  WORLD_STALEST_BRANCH_BURDEN / BORROWED / horizon 21

  BODY_INCOMING / WORLD / horizon 3

  sign 73.33%
  exact delta +19.49

  WORLD_PREVIOUS_FAMILY / BORROWED / horizon 3 / SIGN_BAND
```

Read:

```text
The range layer is not replacing branch memory.
It is acting as the exact-seat confirmation layer when the branch selector can see the family but not the final seat cleanly.
```

Medusa edge separation:

```text
Medusa is no longer below usable exact.
The new EDGE_SEPARATION layer promotes Medusa from FAMILY_USABLE into USABLE_EXACT.
```

```text
DOMINANT_ORIGIN_INCOMING
```

Finding:

```text
For Medusa, this recipe can read signed motion strongly:
about 85% sign on 20 useful calls in the range audit,
and about 86.96% sign on 23 direct sign-probe calls.
```

But:

```text
It does not become the final exact selector by itself.
The stronger exact move is:

EDGE_BURDEN

highest_burden_seat
highest_burden_level
highest_burden_state

```

Interpretation:

```text
Medusa's exact split is burden-side edge separation.
The motion sign matters, but the exact S1/S5 decision improves when the system asks where burden was stored before edge release.
```

## Motion Range And Band Findings

Date:

```text
2026-06-22
```

Added audits:

```text
Motion_Range_Resolver_Audit.py
Motion_Band_Resolver_Audit.py
Motion_Range_Ceiling_Audit.py
```

Output records:

```text
motion_range_resolver_audit_medusa_min2_2015-10-07.json
motion_range_resolver_audit_all_worlds_focused_min2_2015-10-07.json
motion_band_resolver_audit_focused_min2_2015-10-07.json
motion_range_ceiling_audit_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

Core finding:

```text
Outgoing motion amount cannot be treated as solved by branch and sign alone.

The working chain is:

predicted outgoing seat/lane
predicted outgoing sign
predicted outgoing motion band
then outgoing motion range
then current draw lane value + signed range = next draw lane value
```

Why:

```text
Branch + sign gives direction, but the amount still stays too wide.
Branch + sign + motion band collapses the amount into a tight practical range.
```

Ceiling proof:

```text
These are diagnostic ceilings, not live predictions.
They use historical truth keys to show what becomes possible once the live selector can correctly identify branch, sign, and band.
```

Major world range ceiling:

```text
Medusa:
branch+sign width 20 = 51.76%
branch+sign width 30 = 78.89%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 90.91%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Lumina:
branch+sign width 20 = 62.74%
branch+sign width 30 = 79.54%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 92.14%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Citrine:
branch+sign width 20 = 65.17%
branch+sign width 30 = 84.27%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 86.44%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Nova:
branch+sign width 20 = 61.46%
branch+sign width 30 = 78.12%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 92.06%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Suzuka:
branch+sign width 20 = 63.64%
branch+sign width 30 = 77.27%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 94.12%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Circe:
branch+sign width 20 = 56.41%
branch+sign width 30 = 66.67%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 94.12%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%

Artoria:
branch+sign width 20 = 58.82%
branch+sign width 30 = 72.06%
branch+sign+band width 10 = 87.18%
branch+sign+band width 20 = 100.00%
```

Live-safe weakness found:

```text
Current practical range selectors are not strong enough yet.
Focused live-safe amount windows mostly land around 35% to 54% range-hit at width 16 to 20.

That means the exact amount layer is being asked to do too much before the motion band is known.
```

Examples:

```text
Medusa practical focused range:
GLOBAL_COLLISION_INCOMING
BORROWED
horizon 5
SIGN_LOCKED_RADIUS_10
14 calls
50.00% range hit
average width 20

Medusa branch-selected band weakness:
selected useful branch/range room band rate = 14.04%

Medusa live band audit:
selected useful band room band rate = about 29.68%
```

Interpretation:

```text
The money layer is not raw exact number amount yet.
The money layer is motion band / magnitude-state selection.

Once the system knows:

branch
sign
band

the amount range becomes tight enough to calculate the next lane value with real force.
```

Next build target:

```text
Build a motion band / magnitude-state selector by world.
Use current pressure world, authority, burden, pressure topology, incoming sign, transfer family, and prior room memory to decide the outgoing motion band.

Then feed:

predicted branch
predicted sign
predicted band

into the range resolver.
```

Do not do next:

```text
Do not brute-force exact motion amount first.
That will overfit the historical room.
The audit says the exact amount becomes stable only after the band is solved.
```

## World Motion Selector Board

Date:

```text
2026-06-22
```

Added:

```text
World_Motion_Selector_Board.py
world_motion_selector_board_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

Purpose:

```text
Stop treating every pressure world as if it uses the same motion resolver.

Each world now receives its own:

branch selector
sign selector
broad-band selector

The 35-class motion gauge comes after broad band is stable.
```

Board quality:

```text
Branch:
STRONG_EXACT 4
USABLE_EXACT 13
SMALL_EXACT 1

Sign:
USABLE_SIGN 10
SMALL_SIGN 7
OBSERVE_SIGN 1

Broad Band:
USABLE_BAND 7
SMALL_BAND 11
```

Read:

```text
The branch layer is now broadly usable.
The only remaining SMALL_EXACT branch world is Scathach.
The sign layer is healthier than expected.
The broad-band layer is the current bottleneck.
```

Branch upgrade note:

```text
The branch board now treats 5-call exact rooms as usable when the exact/family rates are strong enough.
This matches the current project threshold where low sample is under 3, not under 10.

Small exact dropped:

before: 10
after:  1

Range-confirmation candidates can now participate at 3+ calls, but evidence tier wins before raw percentage.
This prevents 3-call 100% rooms from replacing steadier 5+ call usable selectors.
```

## World Band Preference Audit

Date:

```text
2026-06-22
```

Added:

```text
World_Band_Preference_Audit.py
world_band_preference_audit_min2_2015-10-07.json
```

Purpose:

```text
Use history as behavior evidence for each world.

This is not copying old draws.
It asks:

when this world has this predicted branch,
this predicted sign,
and this current pressure condition,
what broad motion band did history usually allow?
```

Method:

```text
Current rows query memory with predicted branch/sign.
Prior rows store actual branch/sign/band because historical outcomes are known after they happen.

That means the current draw still has to earn the room through live-safe conditions.
```

First audit result:

```text
SMALL_BAND   9
OBSERVE_BAND 5
WEAK_BAND    4
```

Read:

```text
World-specific band preference exists.
The current problem is coverage.

Many of the strongest preference rooms are accurate when they call,
but they only call on a small slice of each world.
```

Selected world preference reads:

```text
Medusa
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / BRANCH_SIGN / h3
5 calls
80.00% band

Rama
COLLISION_PRESSURE / BORROWED / BRANCH_SIGN / h3

80.00% band

Suzuka

5 calls
80.00% band

Nyx
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / FAMILY_SIGN / h13
7 calls
71.43% band

Scathach
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / SIGN_ONLY / h21
5 calls
60.00% band

Alcides
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / BRANCH_SIGN / h5
5 calls
60.00% band

Karna
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / FAMILY_SIGN / h21
5 calls
60.00% band

Altera
AUTHORITY_ORIGIN / BORROWED / FAMILY_SIGN / h5
5 calls
60.00% band

Irisviel

```

Weak or under-covered worlds:

```text
Lumina
2 calls only, despite 100% band on those calls

Artoria
7 calls, 42.86% band

Citrine
0 calls under selected preference room

Nova
0 calls under selected preference room
```

Important interpretation:

```text
This audit improved the explanation layer more than the production selector layer.

It shows which historical situations each world likes,
but it also proves we need broader coverage before this can replace the current broad-band selector.
```

Next build target:

```text
Blend the broad-band board with the world-preference audit.

Use:

current broad-band selector for coverage
world band preference for high-confidence overrides

Then retest:

coverage
band accuracy
which worlds should use preference override
which worlds should stay on the older band selector
```
